





OKWOGERA KWA  MINISITA WA GAVUMENT EZ’EBITUNDU MU BWAKABAKA BWA  BUGADNA NGA KATIKIRO WA BUGANDA AGALAWO ENTEEKATEEKA YA LUWALO LWAFFE 2017 NGA 12/12/2017 (ALIPOOTA YA LUWALO LWAFFE 2017)
PROTOCOL 
Mukama wange Kamalabyano, guno gw’emwaka gw’okusatu okuva  enteekateeka eno  lw’eyatandika mu 2015. Twenyumiriza mu bibala eby’enjawulo byetufunye mu nteekateeka eno omuli bino;
•	Okuleeta ejjamba mu bwa Kabaka bwa Buganda.
•	Okusobozesa abantu b’omutaanda okwegazanyiza mu mbuga y’Obwakabaka.
•	Okuwa omukisa abaami ba Kabaka okuloopa ebifa mu bantu ba Ssaabasajja.
•	Okuwa omwagaanya abantu akumanya agafa embuga n’okulambikibwa ku nsonga ezitali zimu.
•	Eyambye abaami okuggumira mu bantu bebakulembera.
•	Esobozesezza abantu b’Oomutanda okuleeta embuga ebintu ebikozesebwa mu masiro n’ebifo by’obuwaggwa omuli bantu bw’Obwakabaka emmuli, embugo, emikeeka,bibbo,enjulu, obukeedo e.t.c
•	Okunyweza obumu n’obwa seruganda mu bantu ba Kabaka.
•	Okunnyikiza obuvunaanyizibwa bw’abantu eri eggwaga lyabwe.
•	Okuwa omukisa abantu b’Omutanda mu biti byonna okwenyigira mu kukulaakuanya Buganda
•	N’emigaso emirala njoko.
Omwaka guno wabaddewo okweyongera mu bujjumbize bwa luwato lwaffe bwo gerageranya n’omwaka ogwaggwa.
Wetutuukidde olwaleero nga ensimbi 190,707,500= (obukadde kikumi kyenda mwemitwalo nsaanvu mukasaanvu mu bitaano). (Eza Luwalo olwa 12/12/2017 teziriko) zeezaakakugaanyizibwa bwogerageranya ne 137,934,400= ez’omwaka ogwaggwa 2016 . Era n’ebintu bino wammanga bireeteddwa okukozesabwa mu masiro ne mu bifo by’obuwaggwa ebirala;
•	Emikeeka 
•	Embugo
•	Ebibbo
•	Emmuli, obukeedo, n’enjulu, ebiwerera ddala.

ABAKULEMBEZE B’ABAVUBUKA AB’OKWESASULIRA MU BUGANDA BUMU NORTH AMERICA CONVENTION
Oweekitiibwa nkulamusizza nnyo era nkwebaza obuweereza eri Obwakabaka.
Ebbaluwa ekwata ku nsonga eyo waggulu nagifunye, naye  ensonga eno wagimpandiikirako nga 18/03/2019 era nenjaanukula nga 28/03/2019 nga neesigama ku lukalala Oweek. E.L. Ssendaula lweyampa.  Ebbaluwa gyennakuweereza ngitunzeeko kweno.

Ssaabasajja Kabaka Awangaale……….. ng ’Enkumbi ku Bbega !


Kawuki Joseph
Minisita Omubeezi owa Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu, Okulambula kwa Ssaabasajja era Avunaanyizibwa ku nsonga z’Abantu ba Kabaka Ebweru wa Buganda

ABAVUBUKA ABAGENDA MU BUGANDA BUMU NORTH AMERICA CONVENTION
Oweekitiibwa nkulamusizza nnyo era nkwebaza obuweereza eri Obwakabaka.
Ebbaluwa ekwata ku nsonga eyo waggulu ngifunye, era kkiriza  nkutegeeze nti abantu Oweek. E.L. Ssendaula beyampa abaneesasulira bebano  Oweek. Henry Kasakye, Oweek. Ssenkusu Joseph ne Ssentebe wa Buganda Youth Council.

Mukama wange,
RE: OBUKULEMBEZE BW’ENNONO OBWABANYALA
Nkulamusizza Mukama wange era nkwebaza emirimo gy’okolera Obuganda n’okutukulembeera obulungi.
Olwaleero nfunye ebbaluwa okuva ewa MUgerere eya nga 20/05/2019 ngalaga nti Minisita wa Gavumenti ya Uganda avunaanyizibwa ku nsonga z’Obuwangwa egenda kukyaala e Bugerere nga 28/05/2019 essaawa 5:00 ez’okumakya. Era kuno ntunzeeko ebbaluwa evudde ewa Mugerere eraga ensonga zonna.
Mbadde nakagifuna ate Omubaka akikkirira Bugerere mu Lukiiko lwa Buganda Oweek. Ssenkungu Charles Walugendo era ono atera okuleeta ensonga ze Bugerere mu Lukiiko n’okutufunira amawulire genkwe zonna ezikolebwa okufeebya Obwakabaka e Bugerere. Ono akulembeddemu abakaka abalala nebajja mu woofiisi yange bwe babade nga bazze okutongoza olukiiko olunaakola ku lunaku lw’ebyobulamu olugenda okubeera e Bugerere okuva nga 11 okutuuka nga 12 Kasambula 2019.
Ababaka be Bugerere bonna bagamba nti guno gwe mukisa gwebalina okuvaayo okukunga abantu abali emabega wa Ssaabasajja Kabaka bagende mu lukiiko olwo Minisita lwategese balage Namuyonjo omukulembeze ow’Ennono owabanayala era ono Kabaka naye yennyini yamuwa ebbaluwa emukakasa, nabo baanje ensonga zaabwe eri Minisita n’okusaba Gavumenti esse ekitiibwa mu Banyala abagoberera Namulondo.
Ababaka bandaze ne petition gyebateeka ewa Pulizidenti Museveni ku nsonga eno era nayo ngituunze kuno. Bagamba nti ensonga eri ne kumeeza ya Pulizidenti era kyekireeta Minisita.
Nga Minisitule tuwagire  ekiteeso kya Mugerere n’ababaka, nti Obwakabaka busale amagezi mubuyiiya okuyamba Namuyonjo okuteekateeka abakulembeze Babanyala n’abanyala bonna, n’abantu be Bugerere, okwanja ensonga zaabwe eri Gavumenti namaanyi, era mubungi.
 Mukama wange ensonga enno nze enyiinze era ngiwerezza gyoli Kamalabyonna okusalawo ekyokukola, ku nsonga y’okuyamba ku Namuyonjo kuba Buganda bwetamusaamu maanyi talina busobozi ate nga balwanyisa bavujurirwa.
Nze omuwereeza wa Ssaabasajja Kabaka,

Ssaabasajja Kabaka Awangaale!


Christopher Bwanika
Ssaabawolereza era Minisita wa Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu

Kkopi:		Omumyuka wa Katikkiro Asooka era avunaanyizibwa ku nzirukanya
		y’emirimu n’obuyiiya,

Kkopi:		Omukubiriza w’Olukiiko lwa Buganda
Kkopi:		Mugerere.
Kkopi:		Oweek. Ssenkungu Charles Walugendo

ALIPOOTA EKWATA KU BWANAMUYONJO MUSAAZA LY A SSAABASAJJA E BUGERERE  MU BUFUNZE

ENSIBUUKO N’EBYAFAYO BYA NAMUYONJO
Obwanamuyonjo bwatandiikira ku Mulangira  Winyi omubiito okuva e Bunyoro, mu mwaka 1814 yajja n’abantube bangi okwali abakuumi be abalangira n’Abembejja, era nga asibuka mu Omukama Rukidi Mpuga Wasswa mune wa Kato Kimera Ababitto, Abasalibwa Winyi Chwa Male Wasswa e Kibulala Ssingo.  Azalibwa Ssekabaka Kato Kintu ne Nambi , Nambi abaana bano abalongo yabazala bana omulundu gumu Wasswa Winyi Chwa Male, Chwa Nabakka Kato Kasagama ne  Nassolo.
Era okukanya ne kubelawo nakkalirizibwa mu Ssaza lye Bugerere mu mutima gwa tontabalanga mu mulembe gw a Kabaka Ssamakookilo.
Oluvannyuma lwa Winyi okuffa yasikirwa Nayimbwanga, Nayimbwanga, bwaserera, yasikirwa Kwambu Namuyonjo, Kwambu ye yakyusa  embuga ye nagiteka Emisanga Bugerere, NGabweyafa yasikirwa Zagenda Namuyonjo. Wabuula Zagenda yakuuba Embuga ye mu Kitwe Kayooza mu Bugerere era nga naye yakolabingi mu bwa Namuyonjo, Wabula bweyafa yasikirwa Muttali Namuyonjo, omulembegwa Muttali gwasanga obuzibu bungi naddala abazungu bwebamutwara ne bamuwangangusiza Eseesere, ne Jjajawe Kabalega waamu ne Ssakabaka Mwanga.
Oluvannyuma lwokufa obulwadde, yakomezebwawo mu Mbuga ye mu Bugerere nga waano weyafira olwobulwadde obwomusujja obwamukwatira Essesere (Seychelles)
Yasikirwa Omulangira Kalema Namuyonjo, Kalema yatawanamu ne Ssekabaka Daudi Chwa. Ngakiino kyava ku nsonga Ssekabaka Daudi Chwa okutuma abaami okuzimba amasomero mu Bugerere. Olwokutya yaduukira Bukide wabula Ssekabaka yamutuma ng’agamba nti Omulangira tadduka era yakomezebwawo mu Ssaza lya .
Eno gyeyavanga nakiika mu Lubiri e Mmengo, era nga Ssekabaka yasiima nawuwa acre 111 (kikuumi kuminemu) e Banda Galiraya Ebbale. Olw’omukwano gweyarina ne Ssekabaka Daudi Chwa yatuuma ne mutabani we Daudi. Nga  era bweyaserera yasikirwa Daudi Muchwezi Namuyonjo, ono ye yayagalwa nnyo Ssekabaka MUteesa nga yamuwa acres 30 (asaatu) ewabwokwo.  Daudi Muchwezi yasikirwa Mulasa Namuyonjo, eyakuba embuga e Wabinyonyi Bale mu Bugerere. Bweyaserera  yasikirwa Kayemba  Steven  Namuyonjo, nga yabaade Namuyonjo owomulembe Omutebi er a yaserere nga 18/11/2016. Ng’entegeeka  z’okwabya olumbe n’okutuza omusika zigenda mu maaso olwokubawo nga 16/04/2017.
NAMULONDO Y’OBWANAMUYONJO






OMUGAASO GWE ENTEBE YA NAMUYONJO MU BUGANDA
Namuyonjo nteebe yankizo nnyo mu Bwakabaka bwa Buganda, era nga yeemuku masiiga 3 (asatu) nga kwekuli entebe ya Namuyonjo, Nangoma ne Kamuswaga.  Namuyonjo ye mufuzi owensikirano mu Bugerere, wansi w’Obwakabaka ne Ssaabasajja Kabaka. Namuyonjo mufuzi owensikirano e Bugerere nga Kamuswaga e Kkooki.
Namuyonjo yeyatusanga obubaka bwona obwavanga e Mmengo nga era yakiikanga e Mmengo kwogatta n’ebirala ebyenkizo e nnyo. Era nga Namuyonjo ono yarabirwanga Obwakabaka bwa Buganda e Mmengo.
OKUSOMOZEBWA KWE NTEBE YA NAMUYONJO NOKWAGALA OKUMUNAFUYA 
Oluvannyuma lwokujjawo Obwakabaka ekyakolebwa Omumpembe kawenkene Obote, ebintu bingi nnyo byadibangibwa nebyononeeka eby’Ennono n’Obuwangwa mu Buganda, kyokka ate bwebuziddwaawo Mengo tevuddeeyo kuyamba mu kutereza era n’okutegeza abantu mu Buganda obukulu bwa Namuyonjo mu Buganda, n’emikolo  gyakola okutaasa Obuganda, n’okuzimba Buganda eyemaanyi.  Kino kiretedde abagezaako okweyita era neberimbika mu bwa Namuyonjo enkizo okwongera okweyita abafuzi ab’ennono mu Bugerere ate e Ssaza kya Buganda nebatuuka n’okuvoola Buganda yattu.
ERa nga Mmengo bweteveeyo nerambika abantu bayo ab’ennono, bamba nga Kkamuswaga, Namuyonjo, Nangoma n’ebirara bingi nnyo abakyerimbiika nga abafuzi b’ennono ate mu Buganda yattu.  Okugeza nga Baker Kimeze okweyita omufuzi w’ennono mu Bugerere n’okuvoola ekitiibwa kya Buganda, nabalala nga Ssabaluuli mwogeza butamanya okweyita omufuzi w’ennono e Buluuli.
OKUSABA
N’olwensong ezo waggulu, obwa Namuyonjo bufibweeko. Namuyonjo omutuufu atuzibwe ku ntebe y’Obwajjajabwe nga ye mufuzi wesikirano e Bugerere era tewabela wa Ssaza wabula abeera ne Katikkiro , Obuganda bugumire era nenteba ye mu Bulange e Mmengo ebele nga gyeli.
Olwo Obuganda bu beere bumu era bubukare mu mirembe tuve ku benonyeza ebyabwe.

Ssaabasajja Kabaka Awangaale!


Ku lwababiito ne Banna Kabiito
Kayemba Yuuda.






May 9, 2019
Eri: Kabineeti ya Buganda.

ENTAPUTA Y’AMATEEKA N’EMBEERA KU NSONGA Z’ETTAKA LY’OBWAKABAKA ERISANGIBWA MU SSAZA LY’EKKOOKI ERYAKYUSIDDWA N’ERIWEEBWA KAMUSWAGA.
ENNYANJULA:
Mu lubereberye n’okutondawo  ettaka lya Mailo mu Buganda ekyakolebwa mu ndagaano ya 1900, buli wa Ssaza yaweebwa ettaka erirye eryobwannanyini (Private Mailo) wamu n’eryokuddukanyizaako emirimu (official Mailo). Ettaka lino ebiseera ebisinga lyalingako obunene obuweza   Mailo 8 ( omuntu ngafuna mailo munaana ez’obwannanyini ate era nafuna mailo munaana eza woofiisi) . Ettaka  lino lisangibwa mu Ssaza lyennyini ate erimu nga lisangibwa mu bitundu ebirala.
Ettaka lino lya Masaza era emirundi egisinga kwekutudde n’Embuga za Magombolola mu Masaza agenjawulo era nga Embuga ezisinga zituula ku bunene bwa yiika 49. Ettaka ly’Amasaza n’Embuga ez’amagombolola zonna zirina ebyapa ebyawandiisibwa mu mannya g’ebitiibwa by’a bakulembera amasaza n’amagombola agenjawulo .
ENDAGAANO Y’OLWENDA (1900 BUGANDA AGREEMENT)
Mu Katundu 15 akendagaano y’olwenda (1900) engabanya y’ettaka erambikibwa  eri woofiisi zonna ez’Obwakabaka n’abantu sekinnoomu nga n’amasaza kwogatwalidde. Mu ngabanya eno, Kkooki nga erimu ku masaza ga Buganda lyaweebwa ettaka eriwera Mailo 8 ate Kamuswaga ng’omuntu yaweebwa  Mailo 20 (Amakumi Abiri,kubanga ye yali wankizo engeri gyali Omulangira)
EMPANDIISA Y’ETTAKA LINO.
Olwokubanga mu ngabanya y’ettaka , ettaka eryenjawulo lyagabirwa yafeesi ezenjawulo mu Bwakabaka bwa Buganda, waaliwo obwetaavu bwokukola etteeka erisobozesa ofiisi ezenjawulo okuba n’ettaka lino n’okufuna ebyapa mu mannya ga wofiisi ezo. Etteeka lino lyayitibwa Native Official Estates Ordinance Cap 122. Lyakolebwa mu mwaka gwa 1919.
Etteeka lino lyateekawo obwetengeredde (corporation sole) bwa wofiisi ezenjawulo ezaali zifunye ettaka mu ndagaano y’olwenda nezifuna n’ebyapa ku ttaka eryo mu mannya gaazo . Ofiisi nga eya Kabaka wa Buganda, Katikkiro, Namasole, Nalinnya, Omuwanika, Omulamuzi, Abamasaza, Abamagombolola zatandika okuwebwa ebyapa.
Etteeka lyerimu lyalambika nti ettaka lino lya offisi era oyo aliba ali mu ofiisi mu kiseera ekyo yeyalina okuliganyulwamu ate nga bwalikuuma okusobola okuganyulwa oyo aliba amuddidde mu bigere mu ofiisi eyo.
Enzirukanya y’ettaka lino yatambuliranga ddala bwetyo okutuuka mu mwaka gwa 1962 lwewatondebwawo ekitongole kya Buganada Land Board nga kisibuka mu Ssemateeka oyo mu kawaayiro 118. Mu ssemateeka y’omu, waatetekebwawo Federal States ezetongodde era nga buli State yalina ekitongole ekyetongodde okuddukanya ensonga z’ettaka mu state eyo.
Ettaka erisinga ery’amasaza n’amagombolola lyateekebwa mu kitongole kya Buganda Land Board era ebyapa n’ebikyusibwa wadde nga ebyapa ebimu byo tebyakyusibwa.
ENJEGA YA 1966 MU BWA KABAKA. 
Mu katuubagiro akaagwa ku Bwakabaka akaavirako n’okuwangangusibwa kwa Ssekabaka Edward Mutesa II, bingi nnyo ebyakyuka ku ttaka ly’obwakabaka era ssemateeka wa 1962 naggibwawo Gavumenti eyaliko.
SSEMATEEKA WA 1967:
Mu 1967 Semateeka omulala yakolebwa era najjawo Obwakabaka n’obukulembeze obw’ennono obulala.  Mu kawaayiro 108 aka Ssemateeka wa 1967, ettaka lyonna ery’Obwakabaka eryali liddukanyizibwa offisi ez’enjawulo mu Bwakabaka lwawambibwa Gavumenti era neritwalibwa mu Uganda Land Commission. Muno mwazingiramu ettaka lya Kabaka (Kabakaship mailo) ettaka ly’amasaza, Ery’amagombolola, Namasole, Nalinya, Sabaganzi, wamu n’ettaka lyonna erya ofiisi ( Official Estates) Era nga n’ebyapa byonna ebisinga obungi byatwalibwa Gavumenti nebikyusibwa nebiteekebwa mu mannya  ga  Uganda Land Commission.
OKUZZAAWO OBWAKABAKA MU 1993
Oluvanyuma lwa Gavumenti ya NRM okutwala obuyinza, enteekateeka zaakolebwa okuzzaawo Obwakabaka n’okubuddiza ebintu ebyali bibuwambiddwako Gavumenti nga eyita mu Ssemateeka wa 1967.
Etteeka lyakolebwa mu 1993 eriyitibwa The Traditional Rulers (Restitution of Assets And Properties) Act Cap 247 nga ligenderedwamu okuzza ettaka n’ebintu ebirala eby’Obwakabaka ebyali biwambiddwa Gavumenti nga eyita mu Semateeka wa 1967. Okusinziira ku kawaayiro 2 (2), ettaka lyonna n’ebintu byonna ebyali biwambibwa ku Bwakabaka byalina kuddizibwa Obwakabaka  era biteekebwe mu Kabaka wa Buganda nga omukulembeze ow’enono.
Era etteeka lino  lirimu olukalala lw’ebintu ebyaddizibwa  embagirawo.
ENDAGAANO EYAKOLEBWA WAKATI WA GAVUMENTI NE KABAKA WA BUGANDA:
Mu tteeka lya 1993 obuwaayiro 2(5),6,7) bugamba nti ebintu ebirala eby’Obwakabaka biggya kuddizibwa nga wabaddewo okuteeseganya, okukkaanya n’endagaano wakati w’obwakabaka ne Gavumenti era wano wewasibuka endagaano wakati wa Gavumenti ne Kabaka eya 1/8/2013. Endagaano eno yayongera okuzza ettaka ly’Owakabaka nga omwo mwotwalidde ettaka ly’Amasaza era okusinziira ku tteeka lino, ettaka eryo litwalibwa nti likomyewo okuva ku lunaku endagaano lweteekebwako emikono.
ETTAKA LIRINA KUDDIRA ANI?
Ku ntandikwa waasibukawo okukubagana empawa mu bitongole bya Gavumenti nga buli omu yeebuuza nti bweriba nga ettaka ku ntandikwa lyali lyawandiisibwa mu wofiisi eyenjawulo nga Namasole oba Ow’essaza, mu kulizza mu Buganda lyalina kuteekebwa mu mannya ki ? Kino kyaletebwawo embeera nti wetwatuukira mu 1993  etteeka erya  Official Estates Ordinance lyali lyaggyibwawo ( repealed) ate nga amateeka amalala agaaliwo ensonga ya zi ofiisi okufuna ettaka gaali tegagyogerako kubanga enkola ya Federo yali teriiwo.
Ensonga eno yakolebwako ofiisi ya ‘Solicitor General’ wa Uganda mu 2008. Ono mu bbaluwa yalambika ,era n’alungamya  nti ebintu ebiddizibwa mu tteeka lya 1993 tebirina kuddira muntu yenna oba ofiisi yonna okugyako eya  Ssaabasajja Kabaka (The Kabaka of Buganda)  Kubanga mu Buganda  y’etwala eby’ennono mu Buganda.
ETTAKA LY’ESSAZA LY’EKKOOKI
Okufananamu nga amasaza amalala ,Kkooki nayo yafuna  square mile 8 nga okwo kuliko ettaka ly’owessaza ly’ekkooki  (by virtue of his office) wamu  ne ry’Embuga  ezamagobolola . Ettaka lino lyonna  lyakomawo mu ndagaano  eyakolebwa  mu 2013 era okusinziira ku tteeka erikomyawo ebintu by’obwakabaka bitekeddwa  kudda wa Kabaka wa BUGANDA 
OKUKUMPANYA ETTAKA LY’OBWAKABAKA MU KKOOKI.
Twafuna amawulire  nti Kamuswagwa w’ekooki mu lukujjukujju yali akyusa ettaka ly’obwakabaka eriri mu kooki ne mu Kyaddondo okuliteeka mu Kamuswaga w’e Kkooki
Wetwogerera  Buganda Land Baord yakafuna obujulizi obw’ekyapa ekyakolebwa mu lukujjukujju  ku ttaka ly’obwakabaka  eririko embuga ye ggombolola ya Kabaka eya Ssaabaddu  Lwamaggwa  mu Kkooki .
Ekyapa eky’obwakabaka kiwandiise  mu MRV 440 Folio 22 FC No. 25998 acres 49 era nga kiri mu Ssaabaddu w’Ekkooki (BY VIRTUE OF HIS OFFICE) kyakolebwa nga 13/9/1930.  Wabula  ate ekyapa ekyaweebwa Kamuswaga kiraga omukululo ogusibuka mu Ssaabaddu ow’ekooki okudda mu BUGANDA LAND BOARD,UGANDA LAND COMMISSION ate n’ekiteekebwa mu Kamuswaga w’e Kkooki ( The Kamuswaga of Kkooki by Virtue of His Office)
Kino kiraga lwatu nti bwino omu ali ku kyapa kino yasimbulwa  butereevu ku kyapa ky’Obwakabaka  ekiri mu gavumenti  (white page). Tulina n’amawulire nti enkola y’emu yakolebwa ku ttaka ly’Obwakabaka ery’owesazza we Kkooki eriri e Lubaga mu Kyaddondo.
MU MATEEKA KINO EKYAKOLEBWA KU BYAPA KITUUFU?
Okusinziira ku ndaba yaffe, ensobi nnyingi ezakolebwa mu mateeka ku nsonga eno era nga zeezino wammanga;
1.	Ettaka eryogerwako lya bwa Ssaabaddu( Gombolola)  bwe Kkooki   era nga libeera livunaanyizibwako buterevu Buganda kubanga Kkooki lyerimu ku masaza agakola Obwakabaka bwa Buganda .  Essaza lino ligwa mu Disitulikiti ye Rakai erambikiddwa  obulungi mu Ssemateeka wa Uganda nga District ya Buganda. 
2.	Ettaka lino  libadde n’ekyapa okuva mu 1930 era nga ekyapa ekyo kiri mu Ssaabaddu ow’ekkooki   era nga kyekimu kwebyo ebyapa ebyaddizibwa obwakabaka mu 2013
3.	Ekyapa ku ttaka eryo kiri mu mikono gy’obwakabaka  era tewali ngeri yonna ekyapa ekirala gye kisobola  kukolebwamu ku ttaka ly’erimu. Kino ekyapa ekyakolebwa si kya substitute ate si kya Special. Kino etteka n’emisngo egisaliddwa gikikugira.
4.	Ettaka lino ligwa mu ttaka  eryawambibwa ku bwakabaka okuyita mu ssemateeka wa 1967.    Etteeka erikoomyawo ebyawambibwa ku bukulembeze obw’ennono liddiza abo bebawambako ebintu  sso ssi kubiddiza abo abatalinawo mu kiseera ky’okuwamba ebintu. Obwakamuswaga bwa Kooki tebwali bukulembeze bwa nnono obwetengeredde ku Buganda mu 1967. Tewali kyabuwambibwaako mu mbeera eyo n’elwekyo tewali kiyinza kubuddizibwa kubanga etteka liddiza abo abawambibwako ettaka.

5.	 Ensobi endala eyakolebwa kwekuwandiisa ‘The Kamuswaga of Kooki’ ku kyapa. Kino kitegeeza nti yaweebwa enkizo eweebwa Ssabasajja Kabaka mu nnyingo 246 eya Ssemateeka. Kwekugamba Kamuswaga yasuumusiddwa era n’afuulibwa  “ Corporation sole” era  y’enkanankana ne Ssaabasajja Kabaka . Kino kitegeeza nti mu mateeka Kooki eba ekutuddwa ku Buganda.Ssemateeka ku nsonga ya Kkooki yalambika bulungi. Kino kimenya Ssemateeka kubanga ye Ssemamateeka mu First Schedule amenya bulungi disitulikiti ezikola Buganda nga Rakai (Kkooki erambikibwa bulungi) Kino kitegeza nti ekikolwa ekyokutongoza omukulembeze we Kkooki mu  Buganda nga tewali nnongoosereza mu Ssemateeka; kimenya Ssemateeka ate era kisobola okukolebwako kkooti etawulula ensonga za ssemateeka.
KIKI EKIRI EMABEGA W’ENSONGA ZINO?
Tufunye mu bubba ebiwandiiko byonna ebiraga ekkobaane okukutula Kkooki ku Buganda mu lukweesi kweesi ate nga kukolebwa era nekuwagirwa abakungu mu yafeesi za Gavuementi. Kino kirukiddwa nga kirimu okutongoza olulimi olukooki era n’okuluwa ettutumu, okuteekawo radio okukola kino wamu n’okugiwa Omukutu (frequency ey’enkizo ku za UBC). Ebbaluwa ezogera bino zonna zaafuniddwa (zirina okukumibwa nga za kyama) ziyitangana wansi w’omutwe ‘Dismantling of Obwakamuswaga by Mengo establishment’
Ensonga ey’okutongoza obwa Kaamuswaga ng’obukulembeza okwenkanankana n’obwa Kabaka bwa Buganda yatandikira mu Bbago (bill) y’etteeka ku bafuzi abennono n’abensikirano erya 7/12/2010. Ebbago lino lyali liraga obwakamuswaga bwa Kkooki, Obunyala n’obuluuli nga obukulembeze obwetongodde ku Buganda. Wabula kino mu ttteka lyennyini tekyateekebwamu. Wabula mu tteeka lennyini baawagikamu akawaayiro nnamba 6 akaawa minisita w’ekikula kya bantu obuyinza okulangirira n’okutongoza obukulembeze obwensikirano  awantu wonnna mu Uganda. Kino akikola nga ayita mu gazette. Tetunnaba ku kakasa oba nga okutongoza Kamuswaga kyakolebwa mubutongole.  Wabula obubonero bwonna bulaga nti kino bwekiri.
ENDAGAANO YA 2013
Bwetwetegereza empapula ezitambula mu gavumenti abantu bano okukola byebakola byonna beesigama ku kawaayiro nnamba B (iv) akagamba kati
“The Kabaka shall Respect the cultural norms of other related ethnic communities located in Buganda such as Banyala and Baruuli and leave to them land where the former administrative units were situated as was amicably agreed by both parties”
Akawaayiro kano wadde nga tekoogera ku Kkooki bakataputa nti kaawaayo ettaka erituddeko embuga eziri e Kkooki.
Ffe tukataputa nti tekalina kyekaabawa olwensonga zino:
a.	Tewali mbuga gye baazimba yali esobola kubarekerwa. Embuga zonna zaazimbibwa Buganda mu Kkooki nga Ssaza lya Buganda
b.	Tewabangawo kukkaanya wakati wa Buganda ne Kkooki ku nsonga eyo n’olwekyo ekya ….. “as was mutually agreed by both parties”. Si kituufu.
c.	Ebyapa bino mu 2013 byakwasibwa obwa Kabaka era biri mu Buganda Land Board. Tosobola mu mateeka kola nakuwa kyapa kirala ku ttaka lyerimu okuli ekyapa ekirala ekyenkanankana.


EBIYINZA OKUVA MU MBEERA EYOGEDDWAAKO WAGGULU
a.	Essawa yonna Kaamuswaga ayinza okutunda ebitebe bino nga bwebadde enkolaye awalala. Oba okubisinga mu bbanka oba okubigabako liiizi.
b.	Kiyinza okumuwa obuvumu okulumba abaami ba Kabaka n’abakolako ebikolwa ebyeffujjo mu bintundu mwalina ebyapa ebikyuse nebidda mu mannya ge.
c.	Embeera eno etandise okusaasanira ebintu ebirala era nga tufunye n’amabaluwa amalala agatandika embeera yemu e Buruuli mu Nakasongola. Kino era kiyinza nokukolebwa e Bugerere wamu ne mumasaza amalala mu Buganda.
d.	Ssinga embeera eno evaayo mu lujjudde kati eyinza okuteeka endagaano eyakolebwa mu 2013 ku minzaani oba oli awo bannakigwanyizi nebatandika okugamba nti oba oli awo abateesa tebaateeseza bulungi Buganda. 
EKIYINZA OKUKOLEBWA
Ebiyinza okukolebwa bya biti bibiri. Waliwo ebiyinza okukolebwa ku (luuyi) front y’amateeka era nga waliwo nebiyinza okukolebwa ku (luuyi) front y’ebyobufuzi. Wabula ku byombi tekujja kubeerako kitaasiikule nfuufu.
A.	EBYAMATEEKA.
I.	Ebyapa byonna ebyakolebwa tusaba Kabineti ekkirize biteekebweko envumbo. (Caveat) za Ssaabasajja Kabaka. Kino kisaana okukolebwa mu bwangu. Wabula nga kyadikoleddwa ne mu Masaza amalala mwetusuubira nti embeera eno eyinza okubalukawo.  Envumbo eggya kuyamba obutakkiriza Kamuswaga oba omulala kukola kintu kyonna ku byapa nga Obwakabaka tebutegezeddwa n’okukiriza.

Kino kijja kutwala sente nnyingi kubanga kirimu okusooka okunoonyereza Bulooka ne pulooti nga bweziri. Ebyapa ebyatuddizibwa tebiraga Bulooka na Puloti zino. Byatuddizibwa bikyali mu nkola eya MRV system. Kati eyaggalwa. Tusuubira Buganda Land Board esobola okuyambako ku kino.

Tusuubira nti kino bwekinaakolebwa Kamuswaga agya kutabuka era embeera eno tulina okugyetegekera. Wabula okuyisa nokukkiriza caveat zigende ku byapa kiri mu buyinza bwa registrar (discretion) era wayinza okubaawo okusika omuguwa mukyo.

II.	Tuyinza mu mateeka era okuyita mu kawaayiro ak’etteeka eriwandiisa ebyapa. Akawaayiro akawa registrar obuyinza okutereeza register.  Tusobola okumuwandiikira nga tumutegeeza nti yakola ensobi okugaba ebyapa awali ebyapa era n’okukola restitution enkyamu. Kino kitegeeza nti aba alina okugaba notice ya cancellation eri Kamuswaga olwo ne wabaawo okuwozangana mu maaso ga registrar (public hearing).

Kino kijja kuleetera Kamuswaga okuddukira mu kkooti oba okuddukira ewa abo abamuwaga.  Ensonga zijja olwo kudda mu mawulire era kino nakyo tulina okukyetegekera.

III.	Ekkubo eddala eriyinza okukolebwa kwekugenda mu kkooti. Ssaabasajja Kabaka oba yenna gwaba asigidde n’aloopa emisango ebiri. Ogumu mu Kkooti enkulu nga gusaba okusazaamu ebyapa. Mu guno alina kuloopa Commissioner Land Registration wamu ne Kamuswaga n’asaba Kkooti esinziire ku nsonga ezirambuluddwa waggulu esazeemu ebyapa. Nate mu musango guno tuyinza okusabiramu ebiragiro ebiyimiriza Kamuswaga okukola ekintu kyonna ku byapa bino. 

Omusango omulala guyinza okuteekebwa mu Constitutional Court nga guno gusaba okusazaamu okutongoza obwa Kamuswaga. Wano Ssaabasajja Kabaka aba aloopa Gavumenti.

Wabula olwokuba ensonga zino za byabufuzi,ate nga n’obwetengereze bwa Kkooti bubuusibwa busibwa Ebiyinza okuva mu nsala toyinza ku biwaako kakalu (guarantee).

Wabula nebwetutakozesa kkubo ligenda mu kkooti netukozesa ekubo erisooka n’eryokubiri (I. Ne II) Kamuswaga bwetumufunza ayinza okuddukira mu kkoti olwo ekkubo ery’okusatu nnamba III neriteewalika.
B.EKKUBO LY’EBYOBUFUZI.
1. Mulimu okudda ewa Pulezidenti okuteesa ku nsonga eno.
2. Mulimu okutuula ne Kamuswaga n’abalangira ab’enkizo mu Kkooki
3. Mulimu okwasanguza ensonga eno mu lujjudde n’okukunga Obuganda ku nsonga eno
4. Mulimu okuwandiikira gavumenti protest note ku bigenda mu maaso.

OKUKUBIRA.
Ensonga yonna nga bweri tetukyayinza kusirika ne tutabaako kyetukola. Wabula tulina kwetegekera biyinza kuva mu ebyo byetunaaba tusazeewo okukola.


Christopher Bwanika,
Ssaabawolereza era Minisita wa Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu
09/05/2019








April 10, 2019
Oweek. Charles Peter Mayiga,
Katikkiro wa Buganda.

Oweekitiibwa.
OKUSABIRA SSAABASAJJA KABAKA NGA 7/4/2019 MU LUTIKKO E NAMUNGOONA NG’AWEZA EMYAKA 64
Mukama wange nkuyozaayoza olw’emikolo emingi gy’okulembedde era gyokyakulembera ku mazaalibwa ga Bbaffe.
Wantuma okukiikirira Obwakabaka ku nsonga eyo waggulu era obuvunaanyizibwa nabutuukirizza bulungi n’obubakabwo nabusomye era nembuwaayo.
Okusaba kwagenze bulungi era e Klezia ya Orthodox yantumye okukwebaza ennyo olw’emirimu gyonna gy’oweereza Obuganda ate mu ngeri eyenjawulo n’entuma nkusabe otuuse okuyozaayoza kwaayo eri Ssaabasajja olw’okutuuka ku mazaalibwage ag’emyaka 64 ng’alamula Obuganda.  E Klezia yasabye Katonda ayongere okuwa Ssaabasajja obulamu obulungi ayongere okulamula Obuganda.
E Klezia yebazizza nnyo Ssaabasajja olw’okutumbula eby’obulamu n’eby’enjigiriza n’emirimu emirala emingi egiyamba okutumbula embeera z’abantube. E Klezia eyongera okweyama okukwatizaako Ssaabasajja mu mirimu egyo gyonna.
Natutte ekirabo mu kusinza era nenyigidde mu kusonda ensimbi ezokugulira e Klezia ennanga.
Neyanzizza nnyo obuvunaanyizibwa obwampereddwa

Ssaabasajja Kabaka Awangaale……….. n’Enkumbi ku Bbega !

Christopher Bwanika
Ssaabawolereza era Minisita wa Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu



ALIPOOTA KU MUKOLO GW’OKUTONGOZA OKUZIMBA KABUYONJO MU BUTALE BWA KABAKA OMUNAANA (8) EYATUUMIBWA ‘KAMPALA CITY MARKETS WATER AND SANITATION PROJECT’ (KCMW&SP)
Ssaabasajja, omukolo gw’okutongoza okuzimba kabuyonjo munaana (8) mu butale munaana (8) okuli akatale ke Katwe, Namirembe, Mulago, Bwaise Dembe, Makereere Kivvulu, Bwaise Dembe II, Munaku wasiima gugende mu maaso era gwakolebwa mu katale ke Nakulabye ku lwokuna nga 16/05/2019. Gwakulemberwa kitongole kyo ekya Kabaka Foundation.
  
Abantu nga batudde bawuliriza ebigenda mu maaso ku mukolo, Ayogera ye MC Patriko Mujuuka

Okuteekateeka Omukolo
Mu kuteekateeka  omukolo guno, Kabaka Foundation yatuuza enkiiko za mirundi esatu (3) ez’etabiddwamu; aba Rexba Ltd, abakulembera abasuubuzi okuva mu butale bwonna omunana, abavujjirizi aba Uganda Breweries Limited  (UBL) wamu n’ab’ekitongole kya Pulotoko wano e Mengo.
Mu buwufu bw’ebumu, era baafuba okusaasanya amawulire g’okutongoza omulimu guno nga bayita mu kuwandiika amabaluwa n’okuyita abantu ab’enjawulo okwetaba ku mukolo guno. Era nategeezebwako nga Ssenkulu bweyawandiikira Ssaabasajja okumwanjulira enteekateeka yonna era n’okumusaba asiime omukolo okukolebwa mu katale ke Nakulabye era n’okusiima omuntu anaakola omulimu gw’okutongoza. Kabaka Foundation era yakyala ku mikutu gy’amawulire nga CBS 88.8 ne 89.2 FM, Akaboozi ku 87.9 FM, BBS Terefayina, STV ne Delta  TV okwogerera enteekateeka eno.
Olunaku lw’Omukolo
Enteekateeka y’olunaku yatandika ku ssaawa 4 ez’enkya okutuuka ku ssaawa 6 ez’omuttuntu era nga namanyisibwa nti gwalagibwa butereevu ku ntimbe za BBS TV.
Mukamawange nze Musajjawo Christopher Bwanika, nze nali omugenyi omukulu ku mukolo guno, era nawerekerwaako Bishop Prof. Michael Senyimba omuwi wa magezi eri Boodi ya Kabaka Foundation. 
Gwetabibwako abantu bangi naddala abasuubuzi okuva mu butale bwonna. Twafuna abakulembeze okuva mu Gavumenti ez’ebitundu nga bakulembeddwamu Oweek. Joyce Juliet Nabbosa Ssebugwawo Mayor wa Lubaga Division, abakulembeze mu Bwakabaka abakulemberwamu ow’Eggombolola y’omukulu w’Ekibuga Omuky. Kalyesubulwa Ruth, aba Rexba Ltd abakulemberwamu Omw. Sewava Robert, abavujjirizi aba Uganda Breweries Limited abakulemberwamu Managing Director Omw. Ocitti Mark, aba KCCA, Police eyatuwa obukuumi n’abantu ba Kabaka bangi. Kyo ekitongole kya Kabaka Foundation kya kyikirirwa bulungi kubanga; Bishop Michael Ssenyimba eyawummula yaliwo era yaliko ebigambo byeyayogera kubyafaayo bya Kabaka Foundation n’emirimu gyezze ekkola era n’okwebaza Kabaka olw’okufaayo okuyamba abantu be. Mukyala Pamela Batenga yeyakiikirira Ssenkulu era yeyayogera ku lw’Ekitongole. UBL yagabula abatu eby’okunywa (soda).

Okwogera okw’emirundi esatu; okuli okwa MD wa UBL, Okwa Ssenkulu wa Kabaka Foundation n’okwange kwonna nkutunze ku alipoota eno.
 
Omugenyi omukulu Oweek. Chris Bwanika nga ayogera eri abantu ku Mukolo. Amuliraanye ku Kkono ye MD wa UBL Omw. Ocitti Mark

Mu kwogera kwa MD wa Uganda Breweries Limited, yalaga essanyu olwa Kabaka Foundation okukkiriza okukola era nti babadde bakolagana n’Obwakabaka ebbanga ddene. Era wano yatukwasa ‘Dummy Cheque’ ya bukadde bisatu (300,000,000) nga eweereddwa Kabaka Foundation ku mulimu gw’okuzimba Kabuyonjo 4 mu butale buna obusoose. Obutale buno kuliko; Katwe, Namirembe, Nakulabye ne Mulago. Omuzimbi UBL gweyalonda TROPICAL VENTURES LIMITED (Abubaker Seguya) yayanjulirwa abantu era nanyonyola ngabwebi natambula
 MD wa UBL Omw. Ocitti Mark mu suuti eya kikuusikuusi nga akwasa Dummy Cheque Oweek. Chris Bwanika mu suuti enzirugavu.
Oluvanyuma lw’okwogera kwonna, twagenda mu kifo awazimbibwa kabuyonjo e Nakulabye. Mu kifo kino, twasanga bamaze okuzimba omusingi era nga bayiyeeko ne slab. Okwo kwetwazimba ettaaffaali erisooka kyetwatuuma ‘OKUTONGOZA’ twakola bino nga twambaziddwa bulungi mu byambalo ebikozesebwa mu kuzimba.
 
Omukolo gw’okutongoza nga gukolebwa Oweek. Chris Bwanika akutte omwiko n’enkuufiira eya bululu, amuyimiridde emabega ye Mw. Ocitti Mark MD wa UBL.
Abamawulira batubuuza ebibuuzo bingi ku mirimu gya Kabaka Foundation era n’etubanyonyola bulungi ebigendererwa n’ebikolwa byaayo.
Mukamawange ebyakolebwa byonna bizze biragibwa  ku ntimbe za TV ez’enjawulo era ne radio. Mu ngeri eyenjawulo bizze bifulumizibwa ne mu mpapula z’Amawulire. New Vision w’olwomukaaga nga18/05/2019, Monitor ne Bukedde w’olwokubiri nga 21/05/2019 ate ne ku “You Tube” kwebiri
Ebyafulumizibwa mu mpapula ezo zonna mbigasse ku alipoota eno. 

Ssaabasajja Kabaka Awangaale

Oweek. Christopher Bwanika, 
Omuyima mu Kitongole kya Kabaka Foundation/Ssaabawolereza era Minisita wa Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu  







Annex I

Okwogera Oweek. Chris Bwanika, Trustee KF era Ssaabawolereza w’Obwakabaka bwa Buganda mu Kutongoza Omulimu gw’Okuzimba Kabuyonjo mu Butale bwa Kabaka nga 16/05/2019 e Nakulabye 

Protocol;
Tusanyuse nnyo okubeera wano olwaleero ku mukolo guno ogutegekeddwa bannaffe aba Uganda Breweries nga bali wamu n’Ekitongole ekya Kabaka Foundation, ekyatondebwaawo Ssaabasajja yenyini era nga ye Ssentebe waakyo.
Nnina essanyu okubategeeza nti Ssaabasajja Kabaka gyali mulamu bulungi era antumye okubalaba.
Leero tuku??aanye ku nsonga y’akutumbula bya bulamu bwaffe nga tusinziira wetukolera. Obuvunanyizibwa bw’okukuuma obuyonjo bwaffe ffenna, kati bwetuba twogera ku kukuuma obuyonjo, mu bifo wetukolera buli muntu avunanyizibwa ky’enkanyi. Tulina okufuba ennyo okwewala endwadde n’addala eziva ku bukyafu  tusobole okuba abalamu.
Twebaza nnyo Uganda Breweries Limited olw’okuvaayo okuddiza ku bantu baffe n’addala abakolera mu butale era n’abo abaliraanye obutale buno nga etuwadde ssente ez’okuzimba Kabuyonjo 8 mu butale munaana (8) okwetooloola e kibuga Kampala. Mwebale nnyo bannaffe.
Tusuubira nti Kabuyonjo zino zigenda kutumbula obuyonjo mu butale bwa Ssaabasajja bwonna obuli mu Kampala era tusaba abantu baffe naddala abasuubuzi okuwagira omulimu guno gusobole okuggwa mu budde.
Twebaza nnyo aba Kabaka Foundation, Rexba Ltd abakulembeze wamu n’abasuubuzi olw’okuteekateeka omukolo guno era twebaza ab’akatale ke Nakulabye olw’okutukyaza. Mwebale nnyo mwenna olw’okubaawo.
Nebigambo ebyo, mbakutira kulwa Boodi ya Kabaka Foundation nti omulimu tujjakugulondoola era n’ensimbi zijja kukumibwa n’okukozesebwa mu bwelufu (accountability) ate Ssaabasajja atukubiriza ffena abali mubuweereza okukozesa ekitono ekiriwo ate tutuuse bingi, eri abantu (frugality and frugal management) era mikwano gyaffe, Uganda Breweries Ltd  ekikiriddwa omukulu
 Mark Ocitti (MD) tubagumya nti ffe n’ebwotuwa akatono tukkajjamu bingi ebituuka kubantu ba Ssaabasajja era tusaba omukago oguvudde emabega ne UBL gugende mu maaso. Abantu bonna tubakubiriza bawagire nyo UBL era abakozesa ebintu ebiri mu tuluba lyeebyo UBL byekola era byetunda bagule bya UBL kuba abamu kuffe tubizudde nti birungi,  tebirwaaza era tebyonoona mirimu ate era tukolere ku nkola ya “Akuwa naawe gwoowa” ate “Teeka sente wolaba”.  
Nnina essanyu okulangirira nti omulimu gw’okuzimba Kabuyonjo zonna omunaana (8) mu katale ke; Katwe, Namirembe, Nakulabye, Makerere Kivvulu, Mulago, Munaku, Bwaise 1 ne Bwaise Dembe ngutongozza.
Ssaabasajja Kabaka Awangaale

Oweek. Christopher Bwanika, 
Omuyima mu Kitongole kya Kabaka Foundation/Ssaabawolereza era Minisita wa Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu  



Annex II
TALKING POINTS FOR MS. PAMELA BATENGA, AG ED KABAKA FOUNDATION AT THE LAUNCH OF THE KAMPALA CAPITAL CITY MARKETS WATER AND SANITATION PROJECT AT NAKULABYE MARKET ON THURSDAY 16TH MAY 2019
•	Our Guest of Honor, Oweek. Chris Bwanika, the Attorney General of Buganda
•	The Mayor of Lubaga, Oweek. Joyce Ssebugwawo Nabbosa
•	The MD, Uganda Breweries Limited, Mr. Mark Ocitti
•	Retired Bishop Michael Senyimba
•	The CEO REXBA, Mr. Robert Sewava
•	Ow’Egombolola  ly’omukulu we Kibuga, Mrs. Ruth Kalyesubula

Ladies and Gentlemen,
1.	Let me take this opportunity to thank the Guest of Honour and all of you here present for sparing time to attend this function which is of significance to our organisation.
2.	Kabaka Foundation (KF) is an NGO governed by a Board of Trustees chaired by His Majesty the Kabaka of Buganda. The Organisation has over 20 years’ experience in building the capacity of the people in Buganda for sustainable community development. It achieves this mission through the promotion of culture, poverty alleviation, employment creation, environmental conservation, increasing access to health and education as well as promoting the rights of vulnerable groups in the Kingdom;

3.	In 2018, Kabaka Foundation in collaboration with BBS Television started the Omugotteko Programme with the intention of reaching out to the disadvantaged people in slum areas. It was through this Programme that we attracted support from East African Breweries Ltd (EABL) Foundation worth three hundred million (300,000,000/=) for the construction of one eight-stance toilet facility in each of the markets of Katwe, Mengo, Nakulabye and Mulago. The construction of similar facilities in the markets of Makerere Kivulu, Bwaise- Dembe I, Bwaise - Dembe II and Munaku markets will follow in the short run.

4.	This project marks another milestone in achieving Kabaka Foundation’s aim of improving sanitation. Our markets have had old and insufficient sanitation facilities but with the construction of these new facilities, we will  be able to address the problem of poor sanitation and the consequent spread of diseases among the residents, especially the children even better
5.	At this juncture, let me take this opportunity to extend the appreciation of the Board and staff of Kabaka Foundation for the support from the EABL Foundation. As an organization, we pledge to ensure that the facilities are well maintained and remain accessible to the general public including persons with disabilities.

6.	In the same vein, I wish to thank REXBA and the management of the markets for the support rendered to the contractor who is constructing these facilities in the markets of Katwe, Mengo, Nakulabye and Mulago. As a team, we should endeavour to ensure that these facilities are completed in time and made ready for commissioning in July 2019 as is planned.

7.	Before, I invite the Guest of Honour to address this audience, let me invite the contractor to show us what these toilet facilities will look like.

8.	Once again I thank all of you for gracing this event. 

9.	Finally, it is my pleasure to humbly request the retired Bishop Michael Senyimba to invite the Guest of Honor to address this audience and thereafter launch the Project 

THANK YOU




PAMERA BATENGA
A.G. EXECUTIBVE DIRECTOR
KABAKA FOUNDATION

OKWOGERA KWA BISHOP SENYIMBA
Bishop yenyonyolako era nalaga nga Kabaka bweyasiima namulonda okubeera omuyiima wa Kabaka Foundation okuva ku ntandiikwa ate  nawumula naawerezza ebbanga wabula nga Kabaka yasiima namuyita ayongere okuba omuwi wamagezi ku Boodi ya Kabaka Foundation
Yanyonyola ebigendererwa bya Kabaka Foundation n’emirimu gy’ekola, era nalaga nti ekulirwa Ssaabasajja y’enyini era y’eyagitandiika.
Yanyonyola Kabaka Foundation by’ekoze e Wamala nawalala yasiima UBL olw’obuvujirizi era ne yebaza Ssaabasajja olw’okulumirirwa abantu be.

ALIPOOTA Y’OKULAMBULA OKUSOOKA EKIFO AWANABEERA OMUKOLO GW’OKUGGULAWO EMIPIIRA GY’AMASAZA E SSINGO NGA 1/6/2019 
Ssaabawolereza era Minisita wa Gavementi ez’Ebitundu nga ali wamu n’olukiiko oluteesiteesi ku lunaku lwokuburi nga 21/0/2019, balambudde ekifo awagenda okubeera omukolo gw’okuggulawo emipiira gy’Amasaza mu Ssaza lya Ssaabasajja ery’e Ssingo era mu  babaddewo mulimu, ab’ebyokwerinda nga bakulembeddwamu Major Musaazi, aba Pulotoko, Mukwenda n’abamyukabe, n’abolukiiko oluteesiteesi abalala.

Mu kino bekenenyezezza ekisaawe nebazuula ng’emirimo gy’okukikolako gyakatandika era nebakkiriziganya ku nsonga enkulu ezirina okutunulwamamu:
Ekisaawe kyalambuddwa era bino bye bya kiriziganyiziddwako:
a.	Ssaabasajja ajja kutuukira ku nyumba ye Ssaza (Matutuma) ayanirizibwe Katikkiro ne Mukwenda.
b.	Ssaabasajja Kabaka bwanatuuka ku Ssaaza anaalambula amakula.
c.	Ku nnyumba ye Ssaza (Matutuma) walina okutekebwawo Namusu (Mobile Toilet)
d.	Ennyumba y’Essaza Matutuma yetaagisa okufuyira obuwundo (fumigation) mu bwangu ddala.
e.	Olubiri lwetaagisa okukolebwako mu bwangu.
f.	Abagenyi abayite bagenda kugabulirwa awo ku Ssaza nga bakatuuka.
g.	Wajja kuteekabwawo Kabuyonjo (Mobile Toilets) ezetaagisa mu bifo ebyenjawulo ku kisaawe.
h.	Emiryango egiyingira e kisaawe gy’akukozesebwa abantu bamirundi ebiri 
(i)	Omulyango ogusooka gw’abagenyi abalina (VIP NE VVIP’S cards) oluvanyuma bajja kufuna parking beyongerayo mu kisaawe.
(ii)	Omulyango ogw’okubiri gwabo abalina tickets abanaatula mu pavilions endala. 
(iii)	Ssaabasajja Kabaka ajja kuyingirira mu mulyango omukulu oguli e buvanjuba bamujjiiremu ng’atuuse ku kisaawe.
(iv)	Emmotoka za Ssaabasajja zijja kwetooloora zisimbe kuluda lw’omulyango oguli e buggwajuba w’ekisaawe.
i.	Abaganyi abatalina kkadi (Stickers) bajja kusimba emmotoka zaabwe ku Ssaza.
j.	 Wajja kutekebwaawo aba “Pulotoko ku milyango gye kisaawe Ssaabasajja Kabaka n’aba VVIP’S webayingirira era newebanasimba emmotaka zaabwe. Abapulotoko bajja kubeera n’ekukifo ekikulu (Official pavilion) Ssaabasajja wanaatula.
k.	Kkadi zisaana nezigabibwa mu bwangu ddala okusoboseza abantu okweteekateeka.
l.	E kisaawe kya kuggulibwaawo ku ssaawa emu ey’okumakya nga 1/06/2019 wano kyetagisa aba Pulotoko okubeerawo mu budde.
m.	Abagenyi bonna abayite kisaana  bawebwe “Stickers”.
n.	Kyasaliddwawo abagenyi abayite ab’enjawulo abanatuula okumpi ne Nnamulondo obutasukka bisatu (300).
o.	Ttiketi zinatundibwa mu mita ng’abiri (20) okwesulako n’emiryango webanayaniririza abagenyi.
p.	Tujja kuddamu okulambula ekisaawe nga 29/5/2019 okusobola okulaba nga kikoleddwa bulungi era olukiiko lw’abateesiteesi lwo lugenda mu maaso n’okutuza enkiiko okwongera okunnyikiza enteekateeka era ebinavaayo nabyo tujja kubyanjula.
Ebirala eby’okurowoozaako n’okukolako
1.	Wajja kutegekebwawo okusanyusibwa Ssaabasajja ng’omupiira guwumuddemu.
2.	Ssaabasajja Kabaka bwanaaba asiimye anaawubira ku bantu abanaaba bakungaanye ku kiyitirirwa ng’ayingira e Kibuga Mityana n’ekirala ng’ofuluma amakati g’e Kibuga okwolekera ku Ssaza.
3.	Obubaka bwa Ssaabasajja nga Ambassandor wa UNAIDS ku mulamwa gwa sirimu bufunibwe nga bukyali kuba bulina okutekebwa ku mpewo ku kisaawe ku lunaku lw’omumpiira
4.	Ssaabasajja kenyini yasaba ekyenjawulo okulebwa okukwasa e Ssaza ry’e Ssingo ekirabo ky’okuwangula empaka z’omumpiira gwa Jubireewo.
Abasuubirwa okwaniriza Ssaabasajja Kabaka ng’atuuse mu kisaawe be bano wammanga:
5.	Katikkiro

Bulange Mengo.

ENSONGA: OKUWANDIISA KAMPUNI ENESUUBULA EMWANYI, “BUGANDA COFFEE LTD”
Nkulamusizza era nkwebaza obuweereza.
Nkuwandikidde okukutegeeza nti oluvanyuma lw’okusaba kwaffe eri Uganda Registration of Service Bureau (Company Registry) okukasa oba erinnya “Buganda Coffee Ltd” likkirizibwa okuwandiisa kampuni empya, twakizudde nti waliyo kampuni eyawandisibwa mu 1959 mu mannya ga “West Buganda Coffee Works Ltd” nga ate tetunamanyi oba Obwakabaka tebujirinaako kakwate.
Era wano “Registar of Companies“ weyasinzidde okugaana okukasa erinnya “Buganda Coffee Ltd” kubanga lye fananyiriza Kampuni eyo eyaagulwawo edda okujjako nga tufunye olukusa mu buwandiike okuva eri ba nanyini kampuni eyo.
Nkusaba tufuneyo amannya amalala abiri oba asatu agajja mu kitiibwa ky’Obwakabaka getusobola okutuuma kampuni y’Obwakabaka empya nga naffe bw’etukola kaweefube oba tusobola okumanya n’okufuna banannyini ba kampuni ya West Buganda Coffee Works Ltd.

Oweekitiibwa,
EBYAPA BY’OBWAKABAKA EBY’ESSAZA KKOOKI EBYAKYUSIDDWA NE BIWEEBWA KAMUSWAGA
Nkulamusizza nnyo Mukama wange era nkwebaza emirimu gyonna gy’otuusako engalo.
Ssebo ebbaluwa ya Ssenkulu wa Buganda Land Board eya nga 12/4/2019 gyeyakuwandikira ku  nsonga eyo waggulu twagifunyeko kkopi.
Kyenyamiza nti ebyapa ebyaddizibwa Obwakabaka mu ndagaano ya 2013 wakati wa Pulezidenti wa Uganda ne Kabaka byakyusiddwa ne biteekebwa mu mannya ga Kamuswaga naweebwa ebyapa ebigya ngate Kabaka alina ebyapa ebikadde ku ttaka lye limu.
Ebyapa ebipya byakolebwa mu bukyamu mu mateeka olw’ensonga zino wammanga:
Obwakabaka bulina ebyapa ku ttaka lye limu mu mannya ga Kabaka of Buganda nga byebyasooka okuwandiisibwa era etteeka lya Registration of Tittles Act akawaayiro (section) 48, ligamba nti ekyapa ekyasooka okuwandiisibwa kye ky’enkizo, ate akawaayiro (section) 59 ne ligamba nti ekyapa ekyo ekyasooka kiraga obwannannyini obwenkomeredde ate mu kawaayiro  (section) 64 ne ligamba nti oyo eyawandiisibwa okusooka ku ttaka lye limu ye musukkulumu (His estate is paramount). Kooti zitapuse ensonga zino mu musango miigi mungeri eyo.
N’olw’ekyo, tekisoboka, tekikkirizibwa kuwandiisa byapa bibiri ku ttaka lye limu, bwe kiba ekyapa ekyasooka kikyayimiridde. Buganda Land Board eraga nti ebyapa ebyakoleddwa okuweebwa Kamuswaga ku ttaka lye limu tebyayise mu mitendera.
Woofiisi ya Ssaabawalereza erabye ebirowoozo bya Buganda Land Board era ekiriziganya nabyo (BLB) nti ensonga y’ebyapa by’e Kkooki eyinza okukoleeza olutalo olunaaviirako ettaka lya Kabaka mu b itundu ebirala okugenda mu ngeri yemu (It can set a bad precedent which can trigger similar designs in other areas leading to loss of Kabaka’s Land)
Mukama wange, ndowooza nti kyetaagisa okuwakanya n’okusazaamu ebyapa bino mu bwangu nga tuyitira mu mbuga z’amateeka okuzikizza oluyiira luno.  Tusemba ebirowoozo bya Buganda Land Board era ekintu kino kyetaagisa mu bwangu okuweereza okulabuka (statutory notice) eri Ssaabawalereza wa Gavumenti ya Uganda ku nsonga eno nga namakubo amalala Buganda Land Board getesezza bwe gakwatibwa.
Tulabyeko mu nsonga ezifaanana bwe zityo ng’ebyapa ebipya ebikoleddwa ku ttaka lye limu awali ebyapa ebikadde, nga Ssaabawolereza wa Gavumenti eya wakati awa amagezi (Legal Opinions) nti ekyo tekikkirizibwa mu mateeka era tusuubira nti Ssaabawolereza wa Uganda ajjakuwa amagezi ge gamu ku nsonga eno ennene singa tugituusa ku mmeezaye. Ssaabawolereza wa Gavementi ya Uganda bwannaalemererwa okuwabula obulungi, esonga eyinza okwogerwayo mu kkooti ezitaputa amateeka ago.
Ettaka lyetaaga okusibwako envumbo (Caveats) mu bwangu okulikuuma obutatundibwa ng’ensonga bwe zitambula.
Ssaabasajja Kabaka Awangaale ……………….. ng’Enkumbi ku Bbega!  
Nze okussaamu ekitiibwa,

Christopher Bwanika
Ssaabawolereza era Minisita wa Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu

Kkopi:		Minisita ow’Emirimu gy’Obwakabaka egy’Enkizo
KKopi:		Omuwandiisi wa Ssaabasajja Kabaka owekyama
Kkopi:		Ssenkulu wa Buganda Land Board

April 11, 2019
Oweek. Hajj, Dr. Twaha Kaawaase,
Omumyuka Asooka owa Katikkiro Avunaanyizibwa ku Nzirukanya y’emirimu n’Obuyiiya


ENSENGEKA Y’OBUWEEREZA MU KITONGOLE KYA SSAABAWOLEREZA

Nkulamusizza nnyo era nkwebaza emirimu gy’okolere Obwakabaka.

Mu lutuula lwa Kabineeti olw’enjawulo olwaliwo nga 14/03/2019 twasabibwa okutunula mu bitongole byaffe okukakasa ensengeka y’obuweereza, nokukakasa abakozi ate n’okukola ensengeka (Ministry Structure) okugiweereza omuwandiisi ow’enkalakkalira esobole okuteekebwa mu Buganda Kingdom Organogram.

Mu kiseera ekyo Ssaabawolereza yali tanneetegereza kimala woofiisi eno empya ku yye, era yali tanakola nteekateeka ey’emyezi esatu egisooka mu woofiisi eno, ate n’enteekateeka eyomumaaso.

Ssaabawolereza ng’amaze okutereera mu ntebe n’okwetegereza woofiisi eno, akisanze nti kyetaagisa okuteeka mu nkola ekiteeso ekyaleetebwa okuwandiisa woofiisi ya Ssaabawolereza nga woofiisi y’abanamateeka entongole (Law Chambers). Ensonga eyo yali yabagibwaawo Ssaabawolereza eyawummula Oweek. David F. K. Mpanga era yayisibwa mu Lukiiko nga yetaagisa okuggusibwa.

N’olw’ekyo kizuuliddwa nti ensengeka y’obuweereza eyayanjulirwa Kabineeti akatundu ak’okuna (Item No. 4) akakwaata ku woofiisi ya Ssaabawolereza yetaagisa okukyuusibwa okusobozesa woofiisi eno okubeera n’ebifo nga bwekiragiddwa mu nsengeka ya “Organogram” gyentunze ku bbaluwa eno kisobozese okuggulawo woofiisi enzijjuvu (Law Chambers).

Kizuuliddwa nti emisango mingi egiwozesebwa Obwakabaka ate n’ensonga endala ezirina okukolebwaako woofiisi ya Ssaabawolereza era ng’omuntu omu Legal officer eyatuweebwa tamala, wabula twetaaga ttiimu ejjudde okusobola okutaasa Nnamulondo n’okukendeeza ensimbi enyingi enyo ezisaasanyizibwa Obwakabaka ku Bannamateeka ab’ebweru (Costs of external Legal Counsel)

Enteekateeka ey’emyezi esatu egisooka yakoleddwa n’eweerezebwa ewa Katikkiro era tugituunze ku bbaluwa eno okwongera okulaga woofiisi nga bw’eteeseteese. Woofiisi eteekateeka embalirira y’ebyensimbi eya woofiisi ya Ssaabawolereza eyokuyingiza mu mbalirira y’ebyensimbi ey’Obwakabaka 2019/2020.

Mukama wange nga maliriza nyongera okukusaba omuwandiisi ow’enkalakkalira okutulaga ebisenge ebyatuweebwa (Office Space) ku mwaliiro ogusooka wetunateeka Ssaabawolereza Law Chambers, okusobola okugenda mu maaso n’enteekateeka.
	

Ssaabasajja Kabaka Awangaale……….. n’Enkumbi ku Bbega !
Nze akussaamu ekitiibwa,


Christopher Bwanika
Ssaabawolereza era Minisita wa Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu

Bulange – Mmengo era Senkulu wa Buganda Land Board. 

ETTAKA LYA SSAABASAJJA KABAKA E KAWEMPE- JINJA MAWUUNO
Nkulamusizza nnyo Ssebo era nkwebaza emirimu awamu n’obuweereza.
Ensonga z’ettaka lino zizze emirundi mingi mu woofisi ya Ssaabawolereza nga Ssaabalangira y’emulugunya ku kutundibwa kw’ettaka eryo, okugenda mu maaso buli kadde ate mu kubalwanyisa natuuka ne mukkomera Ssaabasajja jjeyamununura.  Ekiffo kino kya nonno era nga kivunanyizibwako Balangira.
Wabula kigambibwa nti waliwo Abalangira abamu abakozesa olukujjukujju okutunda ettaka lino era n’okufunamu ensimbi nga tebafunye lukusa kuva eri Buganda Land Board.
Ssaabalangira yasazeewo okukuba abantu bano mu mbuga okutakiiriza ettaka lino era natusaba tumufunire  ku kkoopi y’ekyapa ky’ettaka eryo.
Nkusaba mu buyinza bwo nga minisita w’obuwangwa n’ennono era nga Ssenkulu wa Buganda Land Board okutawaako ku kkoopi y’ekyapa ekyo kisobozese bannamateeka ba  Ssaabalangira okutegeka empaaba yaabwe obulungi.
Ssaabalangira yatutegeezezza nti ensonga eno yatuuse n’okumuviramu okutiisa okukosa obulamu bwe era kyatuwaririzza okumusabira obukuumi obwawaggulu (Security Agencies of the State) aleme kufuna kizibu oba okutya okulwanirira Embuga y’Obuwangwa eno. 
Tugezezzaako kyetusobola okumulwanirira era amabaluwa gabadde gakuweebwako kkopi
Tetuyinza kutunula ng’Embuga z’Obuwangwa enkulu zimalibwawo era Ssebo nga Minisita akwatibwako obutereevu ensonga eno tugiwereza ku mmeezayo mu butongole nga naye tetuleseeyo ku lwaniirako Ssaabalangira er a n’okuw agira mu byonokola
Ssaabasajja Kabaka Awangaale


Oweek. Christopher Bwanika, 
Ssaabawolereza era Minisita wa Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu

ENTAPUTA Y’AMATEEKA N’EMBEERA KU NSONGA Z’ETTAKA LY’OBWAKABAKA ERISANGIBWA MU SSAZA KY’EKKOOKI ERYAKYUSIDDWA N’ERIWEEBWA KAMUSWAGA.

Nkulamusizza Mukama wange era nkwebaza emirimo gyonna gy’okolera Obwakabaka ate n’okukulisa  obugonvu bwoyiseemu.
Mukama wange, ensonga eyo waggulu, nga Muzigo 9, 2019, nayanjulira Kabineeti  entamputa nga bwewansaba era  gyensabiddwa Omumyuka wa Katikkiro avunaanyizibwa ku nzirukanya y’emirimu n’obuyiiya, okwongera okugikuweereza leero era ngitunze kuno Mukama wange.
Ensonga ya Kkooki  etteseddwako Kabineeti olwareero ngegatiddwa wamu neya Buluuli Nakasongola era Kabineeti nesemba Obwakabaka buse mangu envumbo (Caveats) ku byapa byonna era  buwandiikire omukulembeze  w’Eggwanga ne Gavumenti okwemulugunya n’okulaga Gavumenti engeri endagaano gyemenyeddwaamu ne’bizibu ebiyinza okubeerawo. 
Nsabiddwa era Ssebo,  n’okukuweereza ebbaluwa ref: 01/05/mm/19 eya nga 14/05/2019 okuva mu ba Matovu & Matovu Advocates etungiddwa kuno, ngeraga nti waliwo ayagala okuwawabira Gavumenti eyawakati eyatuwadde notisi, ku nsonga yebyaffe ebitazibwa oba ebitanatudizibwa.

RE: OBUKELEMBEZE BW’ENNONO OBWABANYALA
Nkulamusiza nnyo Mukama wange era nkwebaza emirimo gy’okolera Obuganda wamu  n’okutukulembeera obulungi.
Nga njuliza ebbaluwa eya nga 23/05/2019 ku nsonga eyo, ate era mukama wange n’essimu yo nga 24/05/2019 ng’oyanukula ku nsonga eyo.
Wantegezeezza ku ssimu nti, kituufu ddala Obwakabaka okuvaayo okuwagira Namuyonjo okwa??anga Gavumenti ng’omufuzi ow’Ennono owa Banyala,  n’okuteekateeka Abanyala okwanja ensonga zaabwe mu lukiIko Minisita wa Gavumenti owa State for Gender & Culture Affairs lwategese nga 28/05/2019.
Mukama wange, nga bwe wannambiika, nagenda mu maaso okutegeeza Oweek. James Ssempiga - Mugerere n’Oweekitiibwa Charles Walugendo, bategeeze Namuyonjo nti Obwakabaka bugenda kuyimirira  naye mu nsonga eyo.
Olwaleero nga 27/05/2019 Namuyonjo, Omulangira Yudah Kayemba Namuyonjo aliko, azze mu woofiisi yange awamu n’owandiisi we Bamuwayira Hassan, ng’awerekeddwako Oweek. James Ssempiga (Mugerere) n’Omubaka wa Bugerere mu Lukiiko Oweek. Charles Walugenndo Ssenkungu wamu ne Musajja mukulu Kayondo George 

Wilson okuva e Bugerere. okusobola okutwaala enteekateeka mu maaso,
Tufunye olukiiko mu woofiisi yange wamu n’abakulu abo okutegerera ddala buwagizi ki Namuyonjo bwasuubira okuva e Mmengo? Namuyonjo atutegeezezza nti akubye enduulu ebbanga ddene ng’asaba Obwakabaka okuvaayo mu lwatu okumulaga eri abantu n’ensi nti ye Namuyonjo  era n’okutambula  naye.   Agamba nti ye Bbeene yavaayo  ddala nga Namuyonjo agenda okutuuzibwa ku Ntebe ya Bajjajjabe n’amuwa  ebbaluwa ekiriza olumbe lwabizibwe Omulangira Yoda Kayemba asikire Kitaawe ate ab’oluganda basalewo ku kya Namuyonjo era n’amuwa n’ente olw’omukolo ogwo. Namuyonjo atudde bulungi mu Ntebe ye. (Ebbaluwa eyava ewa Ssaabasajja ngitunze kuno). Wabula Namuyonjo agamba nti talina busobozi mu ntambula n’enneyiisa okuvaayo mu kitiibwa ekimusaanira.  Namuyonjo olw’ennono asabye nti mu kugenda okusisinkana Gavumenti enkya, afunewo entambula asobole okutuukira mu kitiibwa ekimusaanira era bamulabe  nti ye Namuyonjo.
Namuyonjo era asabye awerekerweko n’abakungu okuva e Mmengo okumuwabula ng’ayanja ensonga ze, aleme kubuzibwabuzibwa.  Alina ekiwandiiko kye yabaze ekiraga ennono y’Obwanamuyonjo gye bwava ky’asabye okumulongosezaamu aweeyo mu Gavumenti, kijjewo okubuzibwabuzibwa obo abeeyagaliza entebe nga Kimeze, bye babuzaabuzizzaamu Gavumenti.
Namuyonjo asuubira okutwala bano wammanga mu kibinja ekinaasisinkana Gavumenti:
1.	Omumbejja Zzalwango.
2.	Oweek.  Charles Walugembe (Mubaka) 
3.	JJajja w’Oluggya mwava.
4.	Omuwandiisi wa Namuyonjo Omuk. Bamuwayira Hassan
5.	Omwogezi wa Namuyonjo
6.	Abakungu  babiri okuva e Mmengo (Abakugu okumuwa amagezi mu lukiiko)
7.	Omubaka wa Mugerere
Mu bwangu ddala nkunze Commissioner Harris Lubega ne mu nnamateeka Twaha Mukasa okuva mu Minisitule eno era nga tubadde nabo mu lukiiko lwaffe, okutunula mu biwandiiko Namuyonjo byategese n’okubiringoosa ate era babeere ku ttiimu eneewerekera  ku Namuyonjo enkya nga 28/05/2019 era Ssebo nsaba bavujjirirwe.
Tusaba Obwakabaka okutunoonyezaayo entambula oba  ensimbi  ebinaasobozesa Namuyonjo okufuna entambula okukunga n’okutambuza ekibinja kye okugenda okusisinkana Minisita wa Gavumenti.
Nsaba Namuyonjo aweebwe omutemwa gw’ensimbi nga Shs: 1,000,000/= (Akakadde Kamu) ye atetenkanye bwanaatuusa ekibinja kye okusisinkana Minisita wa Gavumenti.

ENS: OKUSABA OKUKOLA OBWANAKYEEWA MU WOOFIISI YA SSAABAWOLEREZA WA BUGANDA.
Ebbaluwa yo eya  nga 1 Kafuumulamoawu 2019 yantuukako nga 8/4/2019.
Nkwebaza olw’okwagala Obwakabaka n’okuweereza mu woofiisi  eno nga nakyewa.  Nga bwenakutegeeza, nalina okwebuuza enyingiza y’abawereza nga bwetambula n’amateeka g’Obwakabaka ku nsonga eno era nagiweereza ew’Omuwandiisi ow’Enkalakkalira okulungamizibwa.

Nga mmaze okuwabulwa nkutegeeza nti woofiisi yange erina omwagaanya ogwokutendeka ekiseera ekimpi abo abayingira mu by’amateeka  naye nga Obwakabaka tebutikkiddwa buvunaanyizibwa bwangeri zonna obw’okukusasula omusaala oba ensako.

Wabula nga oyo atendekebwa alina okukuuma ebyama, ekitiibwa, n’amateeka g’Obwakabaka.
Mu kkowe eryo nkukkirizza okugya okutendekebwa muby’amateeka mu woofisi eno ng’otwalibwa nga nakyewa okumala ebbanga lya myezi mukaaga okuva nga 01/06/2019.

Osuubirwa okukola ekirayiro ky’okukuuma butiribiri ebyama bya woofiisi eno era n’eby’Obwakabaka byonna. Onowebwanga emirimu gyonna nga woofiisi ya Ssaabawolereza bweneeba esazeewo.

Tulina okusoomoozebwa n’ekifo ekifunda awakolerwa n’ebyokukozesa naye nga bwotoli mupya mu buweereza ekyo gwe tekikusoomooza  era olina okugumira embeera eriwo.

Ssaabasajja Kabaka  Awangaale!


Christopher Bwanika
Ssaabawolereza era Minisita wa Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu

ENSONGA: OKUTENDEKA OMUYIZI SSOZI ZAKARIA 
Nkulamusizza  era nkwebaza obuweereza.
Mpandiise ebbaluwa eno okukutegeeza nti, nga ba Looya tufuna abayizi abetaaga okugezesebwa “Internship” okusobola okufuna obumanyirivu mu byebakola.  
N’olw’ekyo mpandiise okusemba omuyizi oyo waggulu nga aweerezeddwa Islamic University in Uganda Faculty of Law okufuna okutendekebwa. Omuyizi ono mumanyi nga mpitira mu mukaddewe, Hajji Mustapha Bukulu gwenasoma naye e Kibuli Senior Secondary era nga tusula mu kisulo kimu.
Omuyizi ono abadde nnyo mu bukulembeze bwa Nkobazambogo nga yenyigira mu nsonga z’Obwakabaka. Okutendekebwa “Internship” kwa myezi ebiri (May ne June) ng’ayiga ensonga z’amateeka bwezitambula.
Omuyizi ono wamu ne bakaddebe mbategezeezza nti okukkirizibwa okumutendeka tekiteeka buvunanyizibwa bwonna ku Bwakabaka okumusasula ate alina okukuuma ebyama n’okugondera amateeka agafuga emirimu n’ebyama mu Bwakabaka.
Mukumutendeka, naffe mu woofiisi tusuubira okumuganyulwamu mukutuyambako emirimo eginaaba gimuweereddwa.
Ssaabasajja Kabaka Awangaale!

Christopher Bwanika
Ssaabawolereza era Minisita wa Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu

OKULAMBULA N’OKWEKEBEJJA EBYOBUGAGGA BY’ESSAZA SSINGO NGA 30/5/209

Nkulamusizza nnyo era nkwebaza obuweereza eri Obwakabaka.
Nkuwandiikidde okukutegeeza nti Minisitule  ya Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu ejja kutuma abaweereza baayo okwetaba mu lukiiko lw’essaza olw’omwezi ogwa Muzigo 2019 olwalambikibwa okutuula nga 30/05/2019.   Bajja kwegattibwako abaweereza okuva mu bitongole by’Obwakabaka ebivunaanyizibwa ku byobugagga by’Obwakabaka basobole okulambula n’okwekebejja ebyobugagga by’essaza ng’olukiiko luwedde.
Ebyobugagga eby’okuteekako essira bye bino wammanga:
1.	Ettaka okutudde Embuga y’essaza n’ebizimbe byakwo
2.	Ettaka n’ebizimbe ebyali bikozesebwa Mityana District Local Government kati bye baavaamu
3.	Ettaka n’ebizimbe onkwabeeranga ekitongole kya “Works”
4.	Ekisaawe ky’essaza ekyomupiira
5.	Ettaka okutudde Embuga  y’Eggombolola Mumyuka Busimbi n’ebizimbe byakwo
6.	Embeera Pikipiki zonna ezaagabibwa eri essaza ne mu Maggombolola agatali gamu  gye zirimu.
N’olwensonga eyo tukusaba okutufunira entambula (motoka) eneetusobozesa okutuukiriza obuvunaanyizibwa obwo.

Ssaabasajja Kabaka Awangaale………. ng’Enkumbi ku bbega!

Kawuki Joseph
Minisita Omubeezi owa Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu, n’Okulambula kwa Kabaka

ENS: OKUSABA OKUKOLA OBWANAKYEEWA MU WOOFIISI YA SSAABAWOLEREZA WA BUGANDA.
Nkulamusizza nnyo era nkwebaza obuweereza eri Obwakabaka.
Ebbaluwa yo eya  nga 1 Kafuumulamoawu 2019 yantuukako nga 8/4/2019.
Nkwebaza olw’okwagala Obwakabaka n’okuweereza mu woofiisi  eno nga nakyewa.  Nga bwenakutegeeza, nalina okwebuuza enyingiza y’abawereza nga bwetambula n’amateeka g’Obwakabaka ku nsonga eno era nagiweereza ew’Omuwandiisi ow’Enkalakkalira okulungamizibwa.

Nga mmaze okuwabulwa nkutegeeza nti woofiisi yange erina omwagaanya ogwokutendeka ekiseera ekimpi abo abayingira mu by’amateeka  naye nga Obwakabaka tebutikkiddwa buvunaanyizibwa bwangeri zonna obw’okukusasula omusaala oba ensako.

Wabula nga oyo atendekebwa alina okukuuma ebyama, ekitiibwa, n’amateeka g’Obwakabaka.
Mu kkowe eryo nkukkirizza okugya okutendekebwa muby’amateeka mu woofisi eno ng’otwalibwa nga nakyewa okumala ebbanga lya myezi mukaaga okuva nga 01/06/2019.

Osuubirwa okukola ekirayiro ky’okukuuma butiribiri ebyama bya woofiisi eno era n’eby’Obwakabaka byonna. Onowebwanga emirimu gyonna nga woofiisi ya Ssaabawolereza bweneeba esazeewo.

Tulina okusoomoozebwa n’ekifo ekifunda awakolerwa n’ebyokukozesa naye nga bwotoli mupya mu buweereza ekyo gwe tekikusoomooza  era olina okugumira embeera eriwo.

Ssaabasajja Kabaka  Awangaale!


Christopher Bwanika
Ssaabawolereza era Minisita wa Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu

ENSONGA: OKUGAZIYA WOOFIISI YA SSAABAWOLEREZA 
Nkulamusizza nnyo era nkwebaza emirimo awamu n’obuweereza eri Ssaabasajja Kabaka.
Ku nsonga eyo waggulu, nga bwe twalaga mu nteekateeka ya Ssaabawolereza ey’ennaku 90 nga muno mulimu okuteekawo woofiisi entongole  eyabannamateeka (Law Chambers) ey’okuwolereza Ssaabasajja n’ebitongole b’Obwakabaka era nga twetaaga okugaziwa (Expanding office Space) tusobole okufuna we tuteeka  bannamateeka ne bye tukozesa  nga tufuuse Law Chambers.
We twogerera kati emirimu gitandise okweyongera ate nga kizibu okuwandiisa abanaatukwatirako nga tetulina we tubatuuza n’okuteeka fayiro n’ebirala.
Amafayiro n’ebikozesebwa byonna biterekebwa mu woofiisi ya Ssaabawolereza ng’ojjeeko ewatuukirwa (Reception) gye tugabana ne Minisitule ya Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu, buli kimu kyekyusiza mu woofiisi ya Ssaabawolereza era tufunze.
Tusaba okumanya we tutuuse mu kufuna ebisenge ebirala ebyatusuubizibwa olwo ate tusobole okunoonya abantu n’ebintu ebikola okugaziya woofiisi ya Ssaabawolereza.
Tunaasanyuka nga tuddiddwamu ku nsonga eno tumanye we tuyimiridde.

Ssaabasajja Kabaka Awangaale

Christopher Bwanika 
Ssaabawolereza era Minisita wa Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu

Kkopi: 	Katikkiro wa Buganda
Kkopi: 	Omumyuka Asooka owa Katikkiro
Kkopi: 	Omumyuka Owookubiri owa Katikkiro/Omuwanika

ENS: OLUKALALA LW’EMISANGO EGIKWATA KU BWAKABAKA

Nkulamusizza nnyo Nnyabo era nkwebaza Obuweereza.
Ensonga eyo waggulu y’emu kw’ezo zenasabibwa Kabbineeti okuwaako alipoota.
Nkuweereza alipoota ku misango egikwata ku Kabaka n’Obwakabaka nga bwegiyimiridde, oluvannyuma lw’okuginoonyerezako nga bwetwateesa mu nteeketeeka ya Ssaabawolereza ey’ennaku 90.
Alipoota eri mu Lungereza nga lwe lulimi lwa Kkooti era olwanguwa mu kukola alipoota ku nsonga ezo.
Bwendiba nga ngenda okwanjula alipoota eyo gya kugisoma mu lulimi Oluganda olukozesebwa mu Bwakabaka.
Olukalala luyinza okwongerwako bwewanaabayo emisango egizuuliddwa emirala.
Ssaabasajja Kabaka Awangaale!

Christopher Bwanika
Ssaabawolereza era Minisita wa Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu

Twetaaga okulaba “resolutions” ezalonda ba “Directors” abaliko, era ne ba “Signatories” mu Bank. Ate tukebere ne mu Memorandum of Association okulaba byegamba ku nsonga ng’olonda n’okukyusa ba Directors tusobole okubawabula nga bwemwasaba mu bbaluwa eya nga 16/05/2019.

ALIPOOTA ENVANNYUMA KU MUKOLO GW’OKUKUZA AMAZAALIBWA GA SSAABASAJJA KABAKA AG’EMYAKA 64 E NDEJJE S.S.S BULEMEEZI
Minisita w’entabula za Ssaabasajja Kabaka nga ali wamu n’olukiiko oluteesiteesi bakkaanyizza ku nteekateeka ezenkomeredde ez’omukolo gw’Amazaalibwa ga Ssaabasajja Kabaka, okujjako nga Ssaabasajja Kabaka asiimye ekyenjawulo.  
A)	Okugenda  ewanaabeera omukolo
Mu nteeketeeka ezisuubirwa, Ow’essaza Kangaawo Fred Ntege Ssekamere asuubirwa okutikkula akola nga Kaggo Muky. Agnes Nakibirige Ssempa  eggugu ku nsalo ya Kyaddondo ne Bulemeezi esangibwa mu mugga Lumansi ku kyalo Kaserenge.
Ssaabasajja Kabaka era asuubirwa okuwuubira ku bantube abanubbi e Bbombo, wokyamira okudda e Ndejje. Mu bifo bino byombi wazimbiddwawo ebiyitirirwa.
Kabaka ng’atuuse ku Ndejje S.S.S ajja kwanirizibwa bano bokka
•	Katikkiro
•	Oweek. David Mpanga
•	Kangaawo
•	Bishop wa Luweero Dioceses
•	Ssentebe wa Boodi ya Ndejje S.S.S
•	Omukulu w’Essomero Ndejje S.S.S
•	Ssentebe wa Luweero District Omw. Ronald Ndawula
Ku mukolo wa kwanirizibwa bano:
•	Katikkiro
•	Oweek. David Mpanga
•	Omukulu w’Essomero Ndejje S.S.S
•	Kangaawo

1.	Ssaabasajja bwanaatuuka ku ssomero, ajja kuggulawo ekizimbe ekituumiddwa Namasole Irene Druscilla Namaganda   era asimbeko ejjinja. Bishop anaasooka mu bufunze okukisabira.
2.	Ajja kuyingira mu offiisi era asse omukono mu kitabo ky’essomero, essomero lisaba asse omukono ne ku bbaluwa gyebanatimba ng’ekijjukizo mu Kkakkalabizo.
3.	Ebifaananyi bina (Ssaabasajja bwanaaba asiimye)


4.	Ajja kusimba omuti ogw’ekijjukizo mu ssomero lino (Gujja kuba Muyembe)
5.	Ajja kulambula amakula
6.	Ajja kugenda awali omukolo omukulu
EBIRALA
B)	EBIBBO
Ebibbo Ssaabasajja Kabaka ajja kubikwatira mu nnyumba y’omumyuka w’omukulu w’essomero.  Abaana b’engoma , Namasole, ba Nnaalinnya n’abalangira ba kugabulirwa mu nju z’abasomesa bbiri  okuliraana Ssaabasajja wanaabeera mu bibbo.
Kabaka ng’atambula, asaana abeere mumaaso g’abamugoberera bonna ng’abeesudde nga mita emu.  (Ye Maama Nnabagereka oba abaana b’engoma  bajja kutambula mu ntereza ey’embuga)
(i)	Ku somero, asaanye addirirwe abantu basatu;
Katikkiro, Oweek. David Mpanga, n’Omukulu w’Essomero  Ndejje S.S.S  olwo emabega wa bano wabeeyo Kangaawo, Bishop, Ssentebe wa Boodi ye Ndejje S.S.S ne Ssentebe wa L.C.V Luweero District.
(ii)	Ku kittuluze ky’omukolo, okugeza nga Kabaka agenda okugabula Obuganda;
•	Saabasajja era ajja kutambula mumaaso (era mu mita emu okwawukana ku balala Obuganda bumulabe bulungi)
•	Abanaamubugiriza emabega be bano: Katikkiro, Oweek. David Mpanga, Kangaawo n’Omukulu w’Essomero Ndejje S.S.S (Maama n’abaana b’engoma nga bwanaaba asiimye bo basigadde mu ntereza ey’embuga)
C)	Ebifaanaanyi
Basaba Ssaabaajja asiime beekubise ebifaanaanyi bina ku ssomero lino nga bye bino:
•	Abakulembeze b’abayizi
•	Ekifaanaanyi ne Bood y’Essomero
•	Akakiiko akafuzi ak’abaasomerako mu Ndejje S.S.S (abantu bataano) 
•	Abasomesa

Ssaabasajja Kabaka Awangaale………. ng’Enkumbi ku bbega!

ENS:  ALIPOOYA Y’OKUGGALAWO TTABAMIRUKA W’ABAKYALA

Nkulamusizza Mukamawange era nkwebaza emirimo gyonna gy’okolera Obwakabaka.
Mukamawange, nga 8/Muzigo/ 2019 lwari lunaku lw’abakyala era twebaza nnyo Ssaabasajja Kabaka olw’okuggulawo Ttabamiruka ono awamu n’obubaka bweyawadde abantu be.
Entambuza y’omukolo:
Ssaabasajja Kabaka yatuuse mubudde ku mukolo era waabaddewo okukuuma ebiseera mu byakoleddwa. Omukolo gwabadde gwa kitiibwa.  
Wabula bino bisaana okwongera okwekkaanya ku mikolo Ssaabasajja kwabeera.
(a)	 Byonna ebinaakolebwa n’enkyukakyuka ezomuggundu eziba zikoleddwa bisaana okutegeezebwa Minisita w’entambula za Ssaabasajja ate mubudde.  Tekisana Ssaabasajja kumusuulako bintu byatategeddeko kusobola kubisiima bibe mu nteekateeka okugeza:
(i)	Enteekateeka teyalaze nti munaabaamu ebisanyusa, wewawo nga byabadde binyuvu ddala.
(ii)	Ssaabasajja bweyatuuse ku Nnamulondo yasoose kukkalira naasanyusibwa nga ennyimba eziggulawo tezinnayimbibwa n’okusoma essaala.
(iii)	Enteekateeka y’okukola olubaawo Ssaabasajja kweyatadde omukono ogw’ekijjukizo yazze kikeerezi era nekikalubya n’okutereeza ensobi eyalabiddwa mu nsengeka y’ebifaananyi ekya Ssaabasajja nekya Nnabagereka.

(iv)	Kalabaalaba w’omukolo asaana okumanyibwa mubudde ate n’okukwatagana obulungi naabalina obuvunaanyizibwa obwenjawulo era n’okusigala nga ye Katikkiro wagwo. Okugeza bweyasabye Ekitiibwa kya Buganda, eyabadde amuyambako yalangiridde oluyimba lwe Ggwanga era naalutandika.
Wewawo ngeebyo byeyolese, okutwaliza awamu omukolo gwabadde mulungi ddala era twebaza nnyo Oweek. Prosperous Nankindu Kavuma na bonna beyateeseteese nabo omukolo guno.







May 21, 2019

Oweek. Charles Peter Mayiga,
Katikkiro.

Mukama wange, 

ALIPOOTA Y’OKULAMBULA EKIFO EWANAABEERA OMUKOLO GW’OKUGGULAWO EMIPIIRA GY’AMASAZA E SSINGO NGA 1/6/2019 
Ssaabawalereza era Minisita wa Gavementi ez’Ebitundu nga ali wamu n’olukiiko oluteesiteesi bakkaanyizza ku nteekateeka z’omukolo gw’okuggulawo emipira gy’Amasaza e Ssingo ogunaabeera mu Ssaza lya Ssaabasajja ery’e  Ssingo.
Ebinaakolebwa
Omukolo ogw’okukyusa eggugu gujja kukolebwa ku nsalo ya Busujju ne Ssingo e Buwalula wakati wa Kasujju ne Mukwenda.
?	Kabaka anaayanjulirwa amakula
Ebyataagisa okussaako essira mu nteekateeka eno bye bino wammanga:
1.	Kabaka ajja kutuukira ku nju y’owessaza (Matutuma)era anaayanirizibwa Katikkiro ne Mukwenda.
2.	Ssaabasajja Kabaka ajja kuyingirira mu mulyango oguli e buvanjuba bamujjiiremu ng’atuuse ku kisaawe.
3.	Emmotoka za Ssaabasajja zijja kufuluma zeetooloore ziyingire mu mulyango oguli e buggwajuba w’ekisaawe.
4.	Wajja kutegekebwawo Namusu emabega wa Nnamulondo.
5.	Wajja kubaawo kaabuyonjo (Mobile Toilet) okuliraana akasenge k’abazannyi b’omupiira.
6.	Wajja kutegekebwawo okusanyusibwa Ssaabasajja ng’omupiira guwumuddemu.
7.	Ssaabasajja Kabaka bwanaaba asiimye anaawubira ku bantu abanaaba bakungaanye ku kiyitirirwa ng’ayingira e Kibuga Mityana n’ekirala ng’ofuluma amakati g’e Kibuga okwolekera ku Ssaza.
Abanaayaniriza Ssaabasajja Kabaka ng’atuuse mu kisaawe be bano wammanga:
1.	Katikkiro
2.	Oweek. Henry Ssekabembe Kiberu 
3.	Mukwenda
4.	Oweggombolola Mumyuka Busimbi
5.	Ssebtebe wa LC V  - Mw. Luzige Joseph

7.	Hon. Zzaake Francis Butebi
8.	RDC Mityana District
9.	RPC Wamala Region  Police

Offiisi ya Gavumenti ez’Ebitundu yateekateeka olukiiko lw’okusisinkana abaami b’amagombolola wamu  n’abamyuka baabwe ku muganzirwazza nga 25/04/2019, era   ng’ekigendererwa ky’olukiiko luno  kwe kwanjula enteekateeka y’amagombolola wamu n’okuwa alipoota. 
Obubaka okuva ew’Oweek.  Joseph Kawuki 
Yeebaza nnyo obujjumbize n’emirimo gyebakola wamu n’okumwanirizanga yonna gyebaayita nga balambula amagombolola.
Yabategeeza nti obukulu bw’olukiiko luno lwali lwakwongera kubazuukusa  mungeri gyebakolamu obuweereza bwabwe wamu n’emirimo gyabwe.
Yabategeeza ng’abaweereza ba Ssaabasajja Kabaka, okulaba nga bassa essira mu kwekebera mu mirimo gyabwee era nga mu kwekebera  batunuulire bino wammanga:
-	Nemereddwa wa?
-	Lwaki nemerwddwa?
-	Biki byenandikoze okuvvuunuka bino?
-	Baani abayinza okunyambako?
Yabategeeza nti omwaka guno buli omu yetunulire yekka alabe biki ebimulemye era n’okulonda abantu nga bakozi wamu n’okulondoola ebitongole byebatwaala.
Yabasaba obutawamba buvunaanyizibwa bwabannaabwe abalala n’okulaba nga entuuza y’olukiiko etambulira mu buweereza bw’Obwakabaka ate n’okufaayo ku ndowooza z’abalala abakola ebintu eby’enjawulo.
Okuwuliziganya obulungi ne bannamwe ku mutendera gwona paka wansi wamu n’okufayo okumanya obunafu bw’abo bemukolanabo era bayambibwe okubasitula
Okwewala eby’obufuzi wamu n’okututegezaako nga mugenda okwetaba mu by’obufuzi
Yabakubiriza okukwasiza ku bitongole by’Obwakabaka mu kukola emirimo gya Kabaka. 
Obubaka okuva ew’Oweek.  Christopher Bwanika
Yeebaza nnyo obuweereza bwabwe bonna wamu n’okubakubiriza okujjumbira enkiiko zebayitiddwaamu.
Yabakubiriza okukola enteekateeka n’embalirira nga batambuza emirimo gyabwe wamu n’okuteekawo amakakkalabizo webakolera okusobola okutereeza emirimo.
Okufuna okulu??amizibwa okuva mu Minisitule wamu n’okumanya ebiruubirirwa bya Minisitule  ebikulu nga  bagoberera  enteekateeka zaayo  n’okukuuma ettaka okusobola okuzza Buganda ku ntikko.

EBIROWOOZO OKUVA ERI ABAAMI BA SSAABASAJJA ABAMAGOMBOLOLA  WAMU N’ABAMYUKA BAABWE

No.	Ebirowoozo okuva mu abamagombolola  wamu n’abamyuka baabwe eby’enjawulo	Endowooza ya Minisita  Oweek. Joseph Kawuki
1.		Okusaba Ssaabasajja Kabaka abasisinkaneko nga abamagombolola wamu n’okwanjulibwa nga Kabaka alabiseeko eri Obuganda.	
2.		Ebitongole by’Obwakabaka tebyagala kukolagana naffe kyokka bwetubeera mu lukiiko balaga kirala, tebatulabawo bakolagana n’aba L.C  	
3.		Ssaabasajja Kabaka asiime alonde abaami ba magaombolola n’abamyuka abalala kuba abamu baafa, abalala balwadde. Tusaba ebifo byabwe birowoozebweko okukyusibwa.	
4.		Okuzimba kabuyonjo mu kifo ky’ebyobuwangwa e Nakyegalika – Lubajja.  Abantu babeerayo bangi tuyinza okufuna obulwadde obwamanyi 	
5.		Wafunibweewo abakulu okuva mu woofiisi e Mengo mu biseera ebimu batuukenga mu Magombolola okumanya ebifa ku ttaka ly’e Ggombolola kuba wansi eyo waliyo obuzibu bungi okuva mu Buganda Land Board	
6.		Buganda Land Board ewe ab’Eggombolola ya Central Gavementi wakiri yiika bbiri bateekeko ebizimbe byabwe basobole okuva mu bizimbe byaffe era kino kikolebwe buli ewali ettaka ly’Obwakabaka ely’Egombolola ng’ate ebizimbe by’Egombolola wamu ne Lukiiko Hall Centre Gavumenti yabiganira tuyambiddwa tutya?	
7.		Twasuubizibwa okufuna emwanyi omwaka oguwedde naye ekyeeya nekijja nakaakano tetuzifunanga. Nsaba tufunirwa emwanyi ezo kubanga kati enkuba etandise 	
8.		Aba UNRA baakola oluguudo lwa Hoima nebasaba ku ttaka ly’eMbuga, baagala okusasula naye tebamanyi avunaanyizibwa mu kusasula 	
9.		Okwerula empenda z’ettaka ly’embuga n’amagombolola, ate ne liizi eziba zikakasiddwa singa ow’eggombolola amanyisibwako.

EBIROWOOZO OKUVA ERI ABAAMI BA SSAABASAJJA AB’AMASAZA N’ABAMYUKA BAABWE BYE BAAWADDE KATIKKIRO MU NSISINKANO EYA NGA 28/3/2019 MU BULANGE 


No.	Ebirowoozo okuva mu Bamasaza eby’enjawulo	Endowooza ya Minisita  Oweek. Joseph Kawuki
1.		Abategesi b’emipiira gy’Amasaza bakwatagane n’abamasaza mu ntegeke zonna okuviira ddala kuntandikwa	-	Okusobola okutambuza enteekateeka z’emipiira ennungi

2.		Wabengawo okwanukula obubaka mu bwangu nga balina ensonga zebasindise mu bitongole by’Obwakabaka	-	Tekisaana kukandaalirizibwa nnyo olw’ensonga nti wabeerawo ebirina okukolebwako amangu ddala  

3.		Ssente z’emipiira ezigabibwa eri amasaza bazibawe mu bujjuvu sso ssi mubitundutundu nga bwekiri kati	-	Kino kijja kubasobozesa okuteekateeka emipiira mu budde era mu ngeri esaanye

4.		Okuteekawo empuliziganya okuva mu bitongole bya Buganda okugeza nga BLB, NIL, Majestic nebirala wamu ne minisiitule ez’enjawulo	-	Kino kijja okusobozesa abamasaza okufuna ebikwata ku Mbuga
Oweek. Henry Ssekabembe
5.		Wabengawo okwanukula obubaka mu bwangu nga balina ensonga zebasindise mu bitongole by’Obwakabaka	-	Tekisaana kukandaalirizibwa nnyo olw’ensonga nti wabeerawo ebirina okukolebwako amangu ddala  
Eri Baminisita bonna  
6.		Okuteekawo empuliziganya okuva mu bitongole bya Buganda okugeza nga BLB, NIL, Majestic nebirala wamu ne minisiitule ez’enjawulo	-	Kino kijja okusobozesa abamasaza okufuna ebikwata ku Mbuga
Eri Baminisita bonna  n’Abakulira Ebitongole by”Obwakabaka byona
7.		Mu nsisinkano za Buganda Land Board n’abamasaza kisaana basseemu n’abamagombolola 	-	Ndowooza nga n’ekiebe kya  Minisitule kyanddyetagisiza okwetabamu
Ssenkulu wa Buganda Land Board
8.		Buganda Land Board emanyise Buweekula/abakulembeze  ettaka ly’Obwakabaka n’erya Kabaka ery’obuntu erisangibwa e Buweekula wamu n’elyabalangira n’abambejja	-	Okusobola okumanya ekituufu ku ttaka ly’e Buweekula
Ssenkulu wa Buganda Land Board
9.		Okwerula empenda z’ettaka ly’embuga n’amagombolola	-	Kigwanidde Kibasobozese okumanya ettaka lyebakuuma.
Okwogera kwa Ssentebe, Oweek. Noah Kiyimba
Oweek. Noah Kiyimba yategeeza nti olukiiko luno lwayitibwa okusobola okugonjola obumululu obubaddewo wakati w’abawulire awamu n’ekitongole ky’ebyokwerinda. Yasaba abakiise okuleeta ebirowoozo  ebiyinza okusobozesa enteekateeka zonna zikolebwa bulungi okusobola okuweesa emikolo gw’Obwakabaka ekitiibwa.
Abakiise bakubaganya ebirowoozo era bino wammanga byebyasaalibwawo mu lukiiko luno;
1.	Okukola ku Media y’Obwakabaka (Kabaka Press Unit)BBS ne CBS nga bali wansi wa minisitule y’amawulire nga bebakulembedde enteekateeka eno era nga bakirizibwa okutuuka mubuli kanyomero kono okusobola okufuna amawulire agali ku mutindo.
2.	Okukola Media Centre y’Obwakabaka BBS ne CBS nga bakwata ebigenda mu maaso oluvanyuma nebawa emikutu gy’empuliziganya emirala. Kamera zonna ezikozesebwa mu nteekateeka eno zibeere n’ekisenge mweziterekebwa oluvanyuma lw’okukola omulimo era zikumibwe bulungi nnyo.
3.	Okufuna bannamawulire mu butongole abamanyiddwa okuva mu bitongole by’empuliziganya era bakakasibwe gavumenti ya Ssaabasajja. Ekitongole ky’empuliziganya bwekiba kyagala okukyusa ow’amawulire oyo nga kiwandiikirira minisita wa Ssaabasajja aw’Amawulire.
4.	Banamawulire bano baweebwe kkaadi entongole ebalaga nti bannamawulire ba Ssaabasajja Kabaka wabula nga zawuddwamu abasaka mu Kampala n’emirirwano ate endala nga tufulumye Kampala.
5.	Bannamulire bano bategekebweyo omusomo oluvanyuma lw’okubasunsula ogubalambika engeri gyebalina okutambuzamu emirimo gyabwe obulungi.
6.	Obwakabaka bunyweze ekibiina ekikulembera abamawulire mu Buganda era nakyo kiveeyo n’amateeka gaabwe agabafuga kino kisobozese minisitule y’amawulire okubalambika obulungi ng’esisinzira ku mateeka ago.
7.	Okufuna omutindo gwa kamera awamu n’omukwasi wayo nga guli waggulu nnyo. Kino kijja kulambikibwa minisitule yamawulire nga bali wamu nab’ekwerinda.
8.	Olukiiko lwasalawo wakolebweyo “Policy” ku nsonga y’amawulire awamu n’entambula ya Ssaabasajja.

OLUKIIKO OLWATUULA OLWA MINISITULE Y’AMAWULIRE AWAMU N’EBY’OKWERINDA NGA 14/5/2019 KU  BULANGE  MENGO.

Oweek. Joseph Kawuki yategeeza olukiiko luno nti buli Kitongole kirina okuleeta obuvunaanyizibwa bwakyo ku mukolo gwa Ssaabasajja. Era yabasaba okussa essira ku nsonga y’ebyobufuzi nga tutambuza emirimo gy’Obwakabaka wamu n’obutabusa maaso nnono ya Buganda nga Kabaka analambula. 
Abakiise bakubaganya ebirowoozo kwebyo ebyava mu bbago era bino wammanga byebyasaalibwawo mu lukiiko luno;
5.	Okukola ku Media y’Obwakabaka (Kabaka Press Unit)BBS ne CBS nga bali wansi wa minisitule y’amawulire nga bebakulembedde enteekateeka eno era nga bakirizibwa okutuuka mubuli kanyomero kono okusobola okufuna amawulire agali ku mutindo.
6.	Okukola Media Centre y’Obwakabaka BBS ne CBS nga bakwata ebigenda mu maaso oluvanyuma nebawa emikutu gy’empuliziganya emirala. Kamera zonna ezikozesebwa mu nteekateeka eno zibeere n’ekisenge mweziterekebwa oluvanyuma lw’okukola omulimo era zikumibwe bulungi nnyo.
7.	Okufuna bannamawulire mu butongole abamanyiddwa okuva mu bitongole by’empuliziganya era bakakasibwe gavumenti ya Ssaabasajja. Ekitongole ky’empuliziganya bwekiba kyagala okukyusa ow’amawulire oyo nga kiwandiikirira minisita wa Ssaabasajja aw’Amawulire.
8.	Banamawulire bano baweebwe kkaadi entongole ebalaga nti bannamawulire ba Ssaabasajja Kabaka wabula nga zawuddwamu abasaka mu Kampala n’emirirwano ate endala nga tufulumye Kampala.
9.	Bannamulire bano bategekebweyo omusomo oluvanyuma lw’okubasunsula ogubalambika engeri gyebalina okutambuzamu emirimo gyabwe obulungi.
10.	Obwakabaka bunyweze ekibiina ekikulembera abamawulire mu Buganda era nakyo kiveeyo n’amateeka gaabwe agabafuga kino kisobozese minisitule y’amawulire okubalambika obulungi ng’esisinzira ku mateeka ago.
11.	Okufuna omutindo gwa kamera awamu n’omukwasi wayo nga guli waggulu nnyo. Kino kijja kulambikibwa minisitule yamawulire nga bali wamu nab’ekwerinda.
12.	Olukiiko lwasalawo wakolebweyo “Policy” ku nsonga y’amawulire awamu n’entambula ya Ssaabasajja.
